Thirst (Trap)

by pinkpillow19

Summary

Rio Vidal had been working in Hollywood for years. She had done plenty of interviews, but the thirst posts, those were her favorite.

Chapter 1

CHAPTER 1

 

Rio Vidal sat down at her kitchen table with a glass of cannabis infused soda. She swept her black hair over her shoulder as she had misplaced her hair tie. Her brown eyes sweeping the space once more before finally giving up on its whereabouts.

 

Rio’s agent Lilia Calderu, an old woman with more experience in the business than anyone could ever hope to have, had sent her the draft of a script for the interview tomorrow. Rio appreciated being able to preview the content, and this interview was going to be one of her favorites, unhinged. 

 

Thirst Tweets. That’s what the kids were calling them these days. Rio wasn’t particularly old but she wasn’t one of the 20 somethings running around using the latest terms. She smirked as she opened the doc with screenshots of social media post after social media post – all discussing what people dreamt about doing to her. 

 

She skimmed the usernames first, entertained, and then a bit alarmed at the creativity of her fans. She rolled her neck as she scrolled back to the top ready to read. Her eyes flicking quickly over the words, her eyes crinkling. Wow. How many people wanted her to “rail them” or run them over with a car? 

 

She snorted. Sometimes, even when she prepped for these interviews, things had a tendency of slipping from her brain to her mouth. Rio bit her lip as she read a particularly good one and snorted.

 

Oh how she wished they knew that she didn’t want to dominate others, but that she wanted to be dominated herself. She sighed, everyone was always so disappointed with that fact in real life. The fact that the characters she played weren’t much like her real self seemed to really underwhelm people. 

 

She skimmed the next few. 

 

Please Rio Vidal, stab me with a knife.

Please Rio Vidal, drown me in your bathtub.

I know what Rio Vidal can do with my holes...

 

Rio continued to read, her responses coming to mind as she wondered what might be too unhinged for this media outlet. She looked back at the top of the page and saw it was with Rain Media Group and shook her head as she took another sip of her drink. Rain wouldn’t mind her unfiltered responses, they would capitalize on it.

 

She made a few notes, but her eyes froze as she made it to the next post. The profile image seemed to be of a beautiful woman, a very beautiful, mature, woman.

 

Agatha Harkness, @downyourroad: Fuckkkk. Miss Vidal! I want to remain respectful, but how can I when you look like THAT? I don’t want to sound too crazy, but gods, bend me over my couch and spank me already.

 

Rio’s smile widened, she clicked the link to the actual post and navigated to the woman’s profile picture. Her mouth opened slightly. Fuck, she was beautiful. Menopause had hit her with a beauty stick. It didn’t look like she altered much of anything. Maybe there was some light botox or filler usage, but Rio had to admit, the slight lines on her skin really did something for her. She flipped through some photos and took notice of the way this woman’s hands were always dancing in every image. Rio whistled low. Damn, how she would like this woman to bend her over her own couch and show her what those fingers could do…

 

She took another sip of her drink. Agatha , what an interesting name. Sounded witchy, and she loved witchy things. Her eyes glancing around at her decor, she wouldn’t mind adding more flair to her space. Her case of crystals sat prominently near the entrance to her kitchen, a good location for her since she spent a lot of time in this space.

 

Her eyes looked about. While she had been able to afford a home, being a woman of mixed race in Hollywood meant that she didn’t always get paid the same as her peers. Her house was modest and close as possible to where the interviews and studios were located, but it certainly wasn’t the sprawling mansions of her peers. She was lucky she even had a yard at all for her dog. She had thought making it big would mean her art would one day afford her any type of life she wanted, how that had been far from the truth.

 

She leaned back in her chair, tipping it on its feet, something her mother had tried to train out of her at an early age, and eventually had just given up and told her that if she wanted to split her head open, that it would be on her own medical bills. 

 

Her eyes devoured Agatha Harkness’s posts before remembering she was supposed to be working. 

 

She left the page open behind another window so she could come back to it later, and went back to the finer details of tomorrow's press event. Her head tilted when she saw information she had missed. She was going to be creating fake profiles to talk to some of the thirst commentators, her mind drifting back to Agatha, she would be fun to respond to.

 

She finished her drink and closed her laptop. She needed to go to sleep and get her beauty rest for tomorrow– unfortunately with Agatha’s cheekbones in her mind’s eye, she knew when she found her bed, she would be doing very little sleeping.

Chapter 2

Chapter Notes

They meet... online at least :) Enjoy and let me know your thoughts <3

Chapter 2

Rio took her phone back from the security guard as she drove to the designated slot for her parking pass. She parked and took a long sip from her overly sugary drink. People always assumed she took things black, like her soul, but she was a real sucker for sweet things. She rolled her neck hearing it pop more than a few times, last night had been a late one. She had gone back years in Agatha’s profile and the woman surely didn’t disappoint, especially this one two piece swim number, Rio had practically been drooling. 

 

She let out a deep breath and opened her car door, a modest car by any means for someone in her line of work – she didn’t feel the need to splurge, though she did enjoy a good sports car. Her car was… practical. Besides, why blow all your money on a car when you could invest it and grow your net worth?

 

She took one step outside of the car when a young girl ran right into her, knocking her drink out of her hand, luckily not into her outfit. Rio stood there stunned, she waited for the kid to realize who they ran into and start to profusely apologizing when the girl face-palmed.

 

“The visitor’s parking is in the back right corner of the lot.” She grumbled, “Now there’s coffee all over my shoes…”

 

Rio’s eyes widened slightly. “Okay… well…”

 

The girl raised a hand. “Look, this is all fun and games for you, I am sure, but some of us actually work here and don’t get paid much to do so.”

 

Rio looked about. “So…yeah, I totally get the struggle, I really do. I’ve been there, but,”

 

The girl huffed as she brought out her walkie. “I’ll page Carl to come escort you to wherever you’re going.” The radio started to crackle as Rio placed her hand over the girl’s. 

 

“Look kid, there’s no need. I have a meeting with Vic, this door,” Rio indicated with the nod of her head, “13 is where I am supposed to meet her, my agent said…” She moved to unlock her phone when the girl's eyes narrowed.

 

“Vic? Really? And what business do you have with her?”

 

Rio rolled her eyes and started walking, pocketing her phone. The girl followed behind her. Rio speaking, yet ignoring her gaze. “I’m trying really hard not to flip out on you and pull the whole ‘Don’t you know who I am card’ but you are making it so difficult.” Rio rounded on her. “I get it. You’re in LA chasing your dreams, that’s great, some of us do make it and you never will unless you’re a little delusional – maybe even crazy – but you really need to learn the players before one of us gets you fired.” She eyes shifted as a door opened, she saluted coffee girl as she saw Vic walking through the door and waving her over, coffee girl’s mouth hung open as she about shit her pants. “You’re the interview?”

 

Rio sighed as she plastered a smile on her face for Vic, Lilia had been telling her she needed to smile more and as Vic was one of the people she worked with the most in the industry, for press, she knew she wouldn’t mind her trying something new.

 

“Hey.” She leaned forward and hugged the older woman quickly.

 

“Rio, my goodness, what happened to your shoes, they’re splashed in mud!”

 

The black haired beauty cringed a little at herself as she searched for a lie. “Coffee actually. I’m so clumsy.” She saw coffee girl slinking up behind her as Vic cast her a narrowed glance. “Well, get Miss Vidal another coffee! We can’t have her falling asleep on set.” She wove her arm through Rio’s and took her through the set door. “How was the drive in?”

 

Rio snorted. “You would have thought there was an award show this morning, but I made it.”

 

Vic smiled a genuine smile. “Oh you poor thing. You have a bit of a drive too. Well, we have everything set for you and I remembered how you loved gummy worms so I have some good snacks for our breaks. Did you get the posts I sent Lilia?”

 

Rio nodded as her hand was taken and her fingers were wrapped around a new coffee. Coffee girl avoiding her gaze. She softened her tone. “Thanks sweetheart.” She saw, coffee girl practically jump, but she didn’t have time to deal with her now. She took a sip of the cup as her eyes fell on the small set. “Minimal, just how I like it.”

 

Vic swept her arm over the scene. “I wanted you to be the focus.” She showed Rio to her seat and desk. “Will this chair do? It’s my son’s gaming chair.”

 

Rio pressed her finger to the seat. “Perfect.” She moved to sit and pulled herself closer to the table as hair and makeup descended upon her. Vic grabbing a folder and reading a script, her hand flicking in their general direction. “Just a slight touch up,”

 

Rio tried very hard not to move as fingers swept over her face and hair, she noticed with a slight blush that the woman working on her face momentarily froze when she got to her eyes. Rio offered a warm smile and touched her hand lightly. “I like my eyes dark.”

 

The woman blushed and moved to add a bit more black around her eyes when Rio smiled, she knew she could get her number if she wanted, and perhaps she would. Her internal monologue slowing down to silence as her eyes came upon the posts on the laptop in front of her. Agatha. She would get to see her again. As her face was released, she turned and winked at make up and hair and uttered a quiet thank you as her eyes dove back to the screen.

 

Vic walked over, causing her dark eyes to look up. “Okay, so no rules on my end, we can fix anything in post. Let us have it, baby!”

 

Rio tipped her head. “You got it, coach.”

 

Vic barked some orders and more people filtered into the room, Rio was used to forgetting other’s were there with her, it was part of the craft. She waited for the cue and on ‘Action’ she began.

 

“Hey, I’m Rio Vidal, and this is Your Talking to Rio Vidal. Really.”

 

She made an account and read over the first poster's comment, nearly barking out in laughter at reading it over again. “Well, @sandyfeet69, I think you and me could have a good time in the back of your truck. Call me.”

 

Her eyes flipped to the next, reading it out loud. “Rio Vidal could cut off my balls and stomp on them and I would still say thank you.” Rio dead panned the camera as her voice went flat. “I would cut off your balls, Fred.”

 

She let her eyes glide over the next two – delivering some decent one liners when Agatha’s post arrived. She paused, her heart rate picking up, she swallowed the saliva collecting in her mouth and licked her lips, forgetting there were others in the room. She read this one quietly. 

“ Agatha Harkness, @downyourroad: Fuckkkk. Miss Vidal! I want to remain respectful, but how can I when you look like THAT? I don’t want to sound too crazy, but gods, bend me over my couch and spank me already.”

 

Her eyes didn’t lift as she poked her tongue into her cheek in thought. Her mouth lost its filter. “Why don’t you bend me over your couch and we see where the night takes us, Miss Harkness.”

 

She heard laughter from in front of her, her dilated eyes looked up to catch the man behind the camera smirking, before he mouthed ‘sorry’. She raised a hand and gave him a thumbs up, knowing a second later that they would probably do something with that in post, fuck . She shook her head and continued on. She made another account and really hammed it up with the responses, but her brain was split, and the other half of her mind was solely on Agatha Harkness.

 

***

 

Rio sat smoking a joint in her living room, a large air filter promptly on the table, because she may have enjoyed the effects of weed, but she was never going to allow her home to smell like a stoner’s den. She was taking in the notes from Vic today, the woman ecstatic with the content, promising to send a draft over to Lilia as soon as it was done.

 

Her eyes lingered back on the socials she had left open since the night before. Agatha’s post hovering in the background. She looked up her new fake profiles and sighed. Damn, that was some of her best work, but the moment this dropped she definitely couldn’t be found using those accounts. Her fans would go rabid, her phone would blow up from all the messages. 

 

She had her professional socials linked to her assistant’s email and that poor gay boy had seen and read it all. Billy was a good kid. She wished she could take him on as more than an intern, but unfortunately she only could stretch her spending so far. He was an investment in her career and image building, and hoped she would be able to bring him on forever after her next role – whatever that would be. Her income was steadily trending up and up with every project.

 

She bit at her lip as she contemplated it. She did have a lot of fans, if she wanted to, she could get lost amongst them…

 

She opened incognito and pulled up a social media site. She could just create another account. Her finger hovered over the Sign Up screen before she finally clicked. She stared at the account name box, twiddling her thumbs. Something that said Rio Vidal’s fan, not the person herself. She smirked when she thought of the thirst posts.

 

“@RioVidalsWhore.” She clicked enter and it flashed red.

 

“Shit.” 

 

It was already taken. She grunted as she tried again. “Rio Vidal’s Whore… 69?”

 

It flashed blue. She smirked. “Perfect”.

 

She moved to the interwebs to grab a sexy photo of herself and an unhinged one for the banner image. She smiled, she really liked that silly photo, she had been cackling like a crazy person with her best friend at a premier. She leaned back into her sofa and began to follow a few other fan accounts so she wouldn’t seem too crazy, though her page was new and that should be a red flag on its own. She looked back at her page and edited her description.

 

“Rio Vidal can run me over with a horse.” She clicked save and admired her page. It seemed very in line with what she had seen others make. Her fingers hesitant as she looked up @downyourroad, her eyes lighting up in glee as Agatha’s face appeared, reading her bio once more.

 

I’m just a hole for sexy women I will never meet.

 

Rio smirked. What a forward woman, she wondered if she was that way in person. She clicked follow and was surprised with the speed at which the woman added her back. Her eyes were left blinking in shock. So she was online right now.

 

Rio’s stomach started to tighten as she clicked the message, her fingers tapping on her computer as she thought of what to send before she accidentally typed some gibberish, and accidentally hit send. “Fuck.” She muttered as she moved to smack her hand on her forehead. The ping of her computer had her prying her eyes open.

 

@downyourroad: Did you summon me? Lol

 

The words shot straight to Rio’s core. She was in trouble. She started to let her fingers fly.

@RioVidalsWhore69: I’m glad it worked. Though I must admit that’s… not what I meant to say.

 

Her eyes watched as three dots appeared.

 

@downyourroad: I take it you’re after some new Rio content? I haven’t drawn in a few days, I know… how annoying.

 

Rio smirked. How had she missed that she was an artist?

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: Is it terrible to pretend that’s not what I was after?

 

@downyourroad: I suppose not. It is always nice to pretend I’m appreciated for being a real person. Alas we can skip the pretense, good job finding my personal profile. While it’s on brand with my interests I don’t think I linked this page to my art page.

 

Rio got more comfortable. Letting herself lean onto her side.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: I’m pretty good at sleuthing. But I must say, you yourself are quite the vision, my lady… if that wasn’t too forward.

 

Her eyes crinkled as she read the next response.

 

@downyourroad: Oh a charmer! I haven’t gotten a compliment on my beauty in years, I appreciate the attempt. I’m just lucky I appear to be aging well, though I don’t always recognize myself in the mirror anymore. Early menopause symptoms suck. But thank you… Miss RioVidalsWhore69 for your kindness.

 

Rio’s shoulder’s dropped a bit at the woman’s self deprecation – did she not realize how truly stunning she was? Rio shook her head, trying to get them back on track.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: So I read your thirst post for Miss Vidal, I must say, I can relate.

 

Agatha sent back a bunch of laughing emojis. 

 

@downyourroad: You saw that did you? Well, she’s quite the beauty, what’s a girl to do at the mercy of her aesthetic? I’m just a single mom wishing for things I can never have… speaking of I feel like I’ve read every fanfiction out there about the woman. Do you have any recommendations I might have missed?

 

Rio’s heart rate sped up, she was talking about her! 

 

Of course she was… Agatha was a fan. She rolled her eyes at herself. Her eyes reread the comment again and her eyes took in the extra piece of information, quickly disclosed as if it was a throwaway fact, she had a son.

 

Rio sat back, her fingers disappearing from her keyboard. She wasn’t the best with kids, she tried to be kind, but they really did scare her quite a bit. She reached for her joint that lingered in her makeshift ashtray. 

 

Well that was fun while it lasted. But before she could shut down the page, she took a drag of her paper lined stick, letting the smoke out slowly. Her eyes drifted back to Agatha’s conversation. She watched as bubbles came and went, nothing more was sad. She had been having a good time, something that was rare for her. She set her joint down and tapped her foot, there was no harm in continuing to talk to a hot mom, was there? It wasn’t like she was going to end up ever meeting her kid. 

 

She sat back into the couch and pulled her blanket over her lap, grabbing her laptop.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: you’re pretty hot for a mom.

 

The emoji was immediate. A laughing rolling face.

 

@downyourroad: Thank you.

 

A blushing emoji was added a moment later. Rio smirked, she still had it.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: And lucky for you I’m writing a new story, it’s a good one too, it’s Rio’s last character, the agent, with that woman who was a social worker. Real steamy sort of thing. There’s a lot of ass smacking… would you be into that?

 

There was nothing wrong with a little white lie. She was a creative person. She could come up with something if needed.

 

@downyourroad: oh color me intrigued. Tell me more…

 

Rio set her jaw as she reached for some creative inspiration. 

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: It’s them locked in the office all night for a case. They get up to a little fun, chaos ensues, they ruin evidence, Rio’s character is ready to lose her job for this girl…

 

Thankfully Agatha interrupted her writing before she had to continue about this made up storyline… that she was most definitely not about to write for this woman… Was she?

 

@downyourroad: Okay, you have me. Let me know when it’s finished. I hate the suspense of a work in progress. 

 

Rio smiled. 

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: you got it, baby.

Chapter 3

CHAPTER 3

 

Rio sauntered into Lilia Calderu’s office as she stretched her arms high over her head. “So what’s the verdict? Did I lose you as my agent?” She threw Lilia a smile knowing that the woman was always at least entertained by her antics.

 

Lilia tried to suppress a smile. “Rio, you’re a scary bitch.”

 

Rio giggled. “Awe, Lilia, that’s the nicest thing you’ve ever said to me.” As Lilia waved her off, she sat in the chair opposite Lilia’s desk and placed her elbows on top, then her head in her hands. “Did you see that I smiled for you princessa?”

 

Lilia now did smirk. “Yes, though it was a bit… much.” She sat in her chair and leaned back looking Rio up and down. “You’re a lot of work, you know that?”

 

Rio blew out a breath leaning back and letting her arms collapse out to the sides over the top of the chair, her head tilting up. “It’s exhausting being me.” Her face snapped forward a moment later. “Okay, real talk, how was the clip?”

 

Lila’s eyes glanced sideways to her laptop, then back. “You nailed it, baby.”

 

Rio fist pumped the air, “Yes!” Her eyes shifted to Lilia’s notebook. “Now maybe someone will give me another read for something big. It’s…” her voice lost some of its playful edge. “Been a moment.”

 

Lilia reached forward and patted Rio’s hand. “I’ve got a few things in the works, I’ll let you know soon I promise.” Her eyes looked at her locked door. “Sharon reached out.”

 

Rio sat up straighter. “Sharon… as in Sharon Davis of Monument Pictures? That Sharon Davis?”

 

Lilia snickered. “Rio, keep your voice down before neither of us ever work in this town again. Yes, that… woman.”

 

Rio put her finger to her lips, then zipped her mouth shut, waiting for Lilia to continue.

 

“She’s got a project, something groundbreaking, no clue what yet of course. Wants you to read for it.”

 

Rio bit her bottom lip, shaking her head slightly. “They won’t want me Lilia…”

 

Lila knocked on her dark oak wooden desk. “Hey, don’t curse us. She reached out to me. ”

 

Rio ran her hand through her hair. “Just… keep me posted, yeah?”

 

Lilia nodded. Her face softened. “How is Ruffland?”

 

Rio smiled at the mention of her dog. “Weird as his mother.”

 

Lilia smiled. “You should bring him by to play with Benny this weekend, we’re thinking about going to the beach…”

 

Rio opened her mouth to speak but her phone beeped chirpily at her. “What the hell…”

 

Her eyes looked at an account she didn’t recognize before her sober mind started to fill in the pieces. @downyourroad had sent her a message. Her face split into a smile when she heard the older woman sigh.

 

“Rio, sweetheart, what did you do?”

 

Rio looked up as if the teacher had caught her cutting off the girl in front of her’s ponytail… she had never really known how to flirt appropriately, despite how much she had studied social interaction as a child. She shrugged and tried to school her face. “Nothing.”

 

Lilia raised an eyebrow. “Yeah, I’m going to need you to try that again.” She rubbed at her face. 

 

Rio shifted uncomfortably in her seat. “I’m just talking to someone new… that’s all.”

 

Lilia’s hand slowly lowered. “Do you need an NDA drafted?”

 

Rio furrowed her eyebrows and shook her head. “No… it’s…it’s not that serious.”

 

Lilia cast a pointed look in her direction and Rio opened her mouth offended. “She doesn’t even know it’s me….”

 

Lilia just about facepalmed. “Rio…”

 

Rio tapped at the back of her phone. “We’re just… admiring women in the industry together…”

 

At a sharp sigh, and words that Rio practically heard in her head like Lilia had placed them there, she conceded. “Yes, I kinda, met her through that interview thing.” Her eyes took a strong interest in Lilia’s blue waved carpet. Her eyes trailed up slowly when Lilia was silent. “I promise it’s just a bit of fun…”

 

Lilia stood and walked over to her window, gazing out at the skyline of LA. “It’s never just a bit of fun, Rio, not when someone of your status is involved.” She turned crossing her arms. “The very moment she knows it’s you, I need her to sign a waiver.”

Rio closed her mouth and nodded. “Yes, Lilia.”

 

Lilia leaned on her windowsill. “You deserve some happiness kid, but I can’t have you disappearing on me before this big role.” She pointed a finger at her. “It’s a big opportunity for both of us. 

 

***

 

Rio closed her car door as she slipped her phone from her bag, her lips ticking up at the message.



@downyourroad: got any chapters written? Today was a rough day and I could really use some escapism in my life. 

 

Rio’s finger’s stroked at her phone in thought. She needed to guide them away from the story idea, and she was finding that there was a budding curiosity about Agatha’s life under it all.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: What happened?

 

She watched as the dots appeared then stopped, her eyes looking for their appearance, and right before she sent another message they started up again.



@downyourroad: You sure you want the real story? We could just talk about all the dirty things we want to do to Rio Goddess Vidal instead? ;)



Rio’s eyes drifted to the passenger seat in her car. It had been a long time since she had had a heart-to-heart with another human being, even Lilia. Her eyes relocated to her phone and she started typing.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: I mean we can do that as well – but I wouldn’t mind hearing about your day, we’re online friends, right?

 

She waited while she let Agatha contemplate digging up her story, and her body relaxed when the woman started to type again.

 

@downyourroad: Moral of the story is don’t trust beautiful women in power. My… now ex… wife, really took me for a ride. Left me with a son she refuses to claim, a divorce I can’t afford, and moving back in with my mother who views me as the devil’s incarnate. If it weren’t for Nicky I am sure I would be living on the street somewhere, starving to death, or dying of hypothermia.

 

Rio’s chest constricted a bit, even though she told herself this was just some online person she was never going to meet.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: damn. I’m sorry. What is it you do for a living, if you don’t mind me asking?

 

The dots seemed to dance as Agatha replied.

 

@downyourroad: I’m a washed-up theater kid, double majored in theater and scriptwriting, however, there’s not much of that going around in my little backwoods Illinois town. Don’t have the experience either as my wife snatched me up right after graduation. She wanted a housewife so that is what I became. I lived in a big city in her penthouse until six months ago. Never thought she would leave me, but honestly, I should have seen it coming, the writing was on the wall.

 

Agatha continued to write.

 

@downyourroad: It’s impossible trying to explain things to Nicky, where his mother went. She decided since we used my genetic material that in the end he was my problem. He deserves so much more than her.

 

Rio felt tears begin to collect in the corners of her eyes, this was worse than those fans that told you how some small part you played saved their lives. 

 

@downyourroad: To answer your question I work at a hardware store in town. It’s not glamorous and I barely make any money after I scrape together healthcare and food for Nicky, but it’s something.

 

@downyourroad: See why I need your story now?

 

Rio deflated, she took a deep breath and blew it out slowly. Agatha was going through it, if a small story about a character she had played could make things even a little better for her, who was she to not deliver.

Chapter 4

Chapter Notes

here's some more -- hope you enjoy. and let's manifest those wins at the golden globes (and a kick ass second season!)
Sexting here we come.

Chapter 4

 

Rio flopped onto her bed after a long day of interviews and trying to schmooze executives that wanted into her pants. She had hoped Sharon would be at one of the events, but that woman rarely went to these things, she should have never hoped. 

 

She flipped over to her back and stared at the ceiling. Being an actor was exhilarating and thrilling at the best of times, and fucking lonely and suffocatingly boring at the worst of times. Rio needed to find a project soon or she was going to go crazy. Ruffland licked at her foot and she jolted out of her head. “Bro…” She lifted her head and looked down her body at her gimpy-looking border collie, husky mix, the man was one big fluff ball. “I know… you like me being home all the time, but wouldn’t you rather go back and see your buddies? Have pack walkies? Hm?” She flopped back and had the wind knocked out of her when her dog tackled her.

 

“Ow…” her voice whistled out. She caught her breath and smiled. “At least I have you.” The dog turned and jumped from the bed, retrieving his red toy. Rio’s eyes narrowed. “You just wanted a snack?” She sat up taking the toy with an exaggerated eye roll. “I’m glad this is true love for you.” The dog bounced happily by her side as she wandered to her little kitchen to fill the container with cheese and a few bones. Agatha rolled her eyes. What did this woman take her for? An idiot, that’s what this person thought of her. Just because she spent her time soothing her shitty life with expertly woven tales didn’t mean she was that naïve and stupid. This sounded like a terrible fan fiction story – perhaps this was the plot of the one her friend was writing and this was her work shopping if people would actually be interested in reading it. 

 

@downyourroad: so you're a con woman. What did I even get myself into? You have some nerve, I am so not drawing anything for you now.

 

Her online buddy tried again. Attempting to double down. 

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: I can prove it.

 

Agatha huffed. She didn’t need this. 

 

@downyourroad: Save it. 

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: I could send you that voice memo? Or… another photo in the same underwear set that has my face in it? Or… I don’t do live videos but if that would ease your mind we could… or hop on a call?

 

Agatha locked her phone and did end up chucking it into the shower curtains. Nicky arrived at the door, knocking urgently when he heard the commotion. 

 

“Mom? Mom, are you okay in there?”

 

Agatha tried to breathe through her nose. “I’m fine, Nicky, just give me a moment.” She heard her son hesitate, hovering near the door.

 

She knew nothing good could happen to her. She snorted at the cash sitting in her bank account, well it was too bad the woman had sent it to her, she was keeping it. Maybe one day Agatha Harkness would learn to not be so god damned gullible. When she finally calmed down, she opened the door to find Nicky passed out on the bed, she curled around his small body, pressing her face into his hair. She was never ever going to try and do something for herself again. She was done trying.

Chapter 9

Rio groaned, it had been days since Agatha had responded to her. Every message she sent continued to be read but there never was a response. Rio bit the inside of her cheek hard, tasting blood. Why were women like this? Why was she like this with women? Why couldn’t she be normal?

 

She facepalmed her phone and cursed at the pain, okay she was so not doing that again.

 

She looked around her room, what could she do to get Agatha to believe her… She felt her phone vibrate and was disappointed to see that it was just a text from Lilia, letting her know her interview was dropping tomorrow. She sighed, locking her phone before her eyes slid slowly back to the black brick. 

 

Wait.

 

The Thirst Posts Interview.

 

She scrambled for the link. She could send that! She could tell Agatha something she had said in the interview, that literally next to no one would even know about. She opened her messages with the woman and sent the link.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: The interview I did with your Thirst Post, it drops tomorrow.

 

Rio tried to rack her brain for a bit of hidden information. What had she responded with to Agatha’s post? She closed her eyes and started to flip through her memories as best as she could. Agatha had said she had wanted Rio to bend her over her couch… and Rio herself had said…

 

“Why don’t you bend ME over your couch and we see where the night takes us, Miss Harkness.”

 

That was it! 

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: remember how I said in our conversation, ‘what if Rio wanted you to bend HER over your couch’? I said that in the interview! That I wanted you to bend ME over your couch. It drops tomorrow at 11AM, just… watch it, please?

 

She saw that her message was read but there was no response. She closed her phone and grabbed her keys. She needed to hit the gym, she would text her personal trainer on the way to let him know her body needed a few ass kicking sessions before her event.

 

***

 

Agatha's eyes remained skeptical as she saw “Rio’s” recent message. Why couldn't she just block her? It was beyond her understanding. She sat in the bathroom stall at the hardware store, hiding during her shift. She had asked for the next Friday off, and she had debated if she was still going. She had the room all paid for, it would be stupid to waste it. 

 

But on the other hand, it would be stupid to go, now that her stalker knew exactly where she would be. She should have just pocketed the money and run.

 

Rio Vidal’s interview was indeed coming out tomorrow morning, but anyone who followed her closely already knew it was dropping tomorrow, you didn’t have to actually be Rio Vidal to know that. She closed her eyes as she heard Frank, her boss, opening the lady's room door.

 

“This room is for women only, Frank.” She heard the door start to close, then not quite shut all the way.

 

“Come on, Agatha, you’ve been in there fifteen minutes, we have customers.”

 

Her jaw ticked. “I can’t fucking rush my bowel movements, jack ass, it takes the time it takes. Do you want me to poop at the register? Jesus…” she heard the door click shut then as she let her body fall forward onto her legs. What was she going to do?

 

***

 

Agatha had gotten up early, before her mother, and taken Nicky to the park this morning. Where the two had been running around and Agatha had been able to pretend that her life wasn’t a huge pile of shit. They played make believe and Agatha tapped into her acting skills, her son giggling at her antics.

 

“Momma, use your purple!”

 

Agatha moved her hands in a swirling motion before pretending to throw blasts at her son as he shrieked ducking down across a rickety bridge. Just as she was going to begin her monologue against her prince, her phone alarm sounded, her nerves getting the best of her.

 

“Nicky…Nicky, come down here. We need to go.”

 

Her son’s eyes narrowed in thought as he contemplated arguing. His eyes zeroed in on something as he sighed and walked back down the playset to her. Her eyes wide in shock. Her son rolled his eyes and grabbed her hand.

 

“Your hands are shaking.” He started to pull her along on the walk home. “You didn’t tell me you didn’t feel well, Momma, we could have gone home earlier.”

 

Agatha looked behind her at the park. They had been having a good time, did she really need to watch this interview and see if the response the woman had told her was true? After all, this woman could have been someone from the crew that had knowledge of the interview and still wanted to use her for nefarious reasons.

 

Nicky sighed loudly. “Momma, it’s fine, we can go back to the park tomorrow.”

 

Agatha turned her analytical gaze on her son. “I’m not sick, Nicholas.” She never used his full name, that was reserved for his other mother, a woman who was always far too hard on him. That had to do with her presence no doubt. She sighed as she lightly encouraged Nicky forward. “Go help your grandmother, I have to go check on something.”

 

Nicky turned his little eyes to her. “Is it about…” his voice dipped low. “About mommy?”

 

Agatha took an unconscious step back. “No, Nicky. It’s… not about her.” She waited for more questions but her son nodded as he let her hand fall and he wandered off, like she had asked. She took off her dark jacket and placed it on the hook by her door, her hands rubbing quickly to heat themselves up before she turned on the space heater for warmth. She pulled out her laptop and clicked on the link she had saved from her online friend… well ex-friend.

 

She watched as a countdown initiated for the premier of the video, she had made it back just in time. As the screen dimmed, it was just as quickly replaced with Rio’s smile. 

 

“Hey, I’m Rio Vidal, and this is You’re Talking to Rio Vidal. Really.”

 

Agatha rolled her eyes, okay this was a bit on the nose. She watched as posts were brought up and she felt a bit self conscious with the fact that hers was coming. She didn’t know how actors watched themselves in playback, because she was wanting to crawl out of her skin waiting to hear some words she had thoughtlessly typed and sent out for the whole internet to see.

 

She watched as Rio’s signature charm came forward as she had fun, enjoying the game she was playing with these posts. Finally, Agatha’s post came up and she felt her breath catch as Rio began to read.

 

“ Agatha Harkness, @downyourroad: Fuckkkk. Miss Vidal! I want to remain respectful, but how can I when you look like THAT? I don’t want to sound too crazy, but gods, bend me over my couch and spank me already.”

 

Her eyes didn’t lift as she poked her tongue into her cheek in thought. Her mouth lost its filter. “Why don’t you bend me over your couch and we see where the night takes us, Miss Harkness.” Her eyebrow raised expertly.

 

Agatha’s heart stopped. What had the mystery woman said exactly? She flipped back to the messages and read the words line for line. Her eyes flashing between her phone and the computer quite a few times. 

 

There was no fucking way.

 

***

 

Agatha’s phone lit up with a message. She had been trying to occupy her mind since watching the interview. Trouble was all she did was find a whole bunch of mediocre fanfiction stories online and none of them were doing it for her.

 

She pouted, why was this woman trying so hard to talk to her? Why create this elaborate scheme when Agatha had already enjoyed talking to her? As well as agreeing to meet her in Chicago…

 

She picked up her phone, resigned to having a conversation with the woman finally.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: So… did you watch it yet? It’s out.

 

Agatha let her eyes drift to her laptop. She had watched it twice actually.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: Is this about me lying to you? Because that’s fair. I just… I can’t really go around, like, announcing myself all of the time. That doesn’t go well for me… well, apparently, neither did this.

 

Bright blue eyes scanned the message, looking for hidden meanings, when she came up empty, she started to finally compose a message.

 

@downyourroad: You expect me to believe you, after the fact that there were probably at least 20 people working on that set? You could be anyone.

 

She practically felt the charged energy between her and the other woman waft through her screen.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: There were only seven, actually. Me, Vic, the camera guy, hair, makeup, the DP, and Vic’s intern. It was a small production, just like I prefer.

 

Agatha scoffed, this woman was laying it on thick with the details.

 

@downyourroad: Nevertheless, this is an elaborate joke. What do you get out of it at the end of the day? My suffering? I’ve told you my life is hell and… well I know no one cares, but I thought I at least held some value in my photos.

 

She felt her stomach drop. What value? She was aging, her ex-wife didn’t want her either.

 

The response was slow this time as the woman seemed to have a lot to say.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: Agatha, I’m not trying to do something terrible. I just really enjoy spending time with you on here and I thought that maybe… we might hit it off in real life. I’m in Chicago for a convention. Look it up – I go on Friday morning, then I am free the rest of the weekend. Did you… want me to use a code word in the panel? I know plenty of fans will be recording and uploading it right after. Would that ease your mind?

 

Blue eyes darted away from her phone. What could the woman even say that wouldn’t be used in conversation. As if on cue – fake Rio had a suggestion. 

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: How about Te Veo?

 

Agatha’s eyes glanced over the Spanish. She had taken a brief course at one point, but she certainly didn’t remember what the two words meant. Language wasn’t her strong suit, she only remembered a few phrases at best. Her mood slipped easily into her words.

 

@downyourroad: What the hell does that even mean?

 

She saw the bubbles appear then disappear, but only for a moment.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: It’s a bit hard to explain, languages function a bit differently from each other. I’m bilingual since I’m part Puerto Rican, but essentially… It means I see you. But it’s deeper than just the physical. It’s like I see your soul, that sort of thing.

 

Agatha’s heart hurt. Why would this woman suggest such a phrase?

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: I’ll use it, you’ll see. Will you come to the city? Just in case I do?

 

Agatha wared with herself. Not only did she not want to be disappointed, but she also was becoming increasingly terrified that maybe the woman on the other end of this conversation might be exactly who she said she was.

 

@downyourroad: I’ll consider it.

Chapter 10

Agatha couldn’t quite speak around the lump in her throat, so she nodded and leaned down to kiss him once more. Agatha had never really been away from Nicky before, more than a few hours for work. “Be good for grandma.”

 

Nicky reached up and bopped her on the nose. “For good luck!”

 

Agatha ruffled his hair as her eyes lifted to her mother’s, the woman’s arms were crossed and her face set in a hard glare. “I don’t think moving to Chicago would be the best idea for Nicolas. There’s so much sin and filth there, Agatha…” Her eyes looked her up and down in disgust. “You would know.”

 

Agatha gripped her duffle. “They sent me gas money, and a hotel reservation. Mom, I need to at least… hear them out. You never know, plus, I can’t work at the hardware store forever…”

 

Her mother stepped forward sighing. “Agatha, you need to stop wasting your time and marry a decent man. Nicky needs a father, and then there would be no need for you to be whoring yourself out…”

 

Agatha growled. “No. Nicky doesn’t need a father, mother.” She clenched her fists. “He was born from two women…” The distinction mattered to her. Evanora rolled her eyes. “In the eyes of God, Agatha.” As if her daughter should realize the world of man was full of lies and sin and that the true word could only be found in an old dusty book, written by uneducated men. 

 

Agatha opened the door as her mother ground out a last minute attempt to make her daughter rethink her quest. “You should just leave Nicky with me if you move, he deserves so much more than you.”

 

Her vision blurred. She didn’t remember leaving and she didn’t stop moving until she got in her car and locked the doors. The worst thing was that she believed her mother was right. That Nicky did deserve so much better than her.

 

***

 

Rio sipped at an energy drink as she waited to go on stage. Her eyes flicking around at the commotion behind the curtains. She was in a single panel this morning, it was just thirty minutes with her and the fans, answering questions. She took another sip and checked her phone again. She had no idea if Agatha had made it to the city, she had been buzzing with energy ever since she got on the plane for her red-eye this morning. She was trying to be hopeful that she wouldn’t be stood up, cause that would just suck .  

 

She closed her eyes and tried to breathe. It would be fine, either she would meet Agatha after this, or she wouldn’t. She would be okay, wouldn’t she? Her eyes opened as she heard her name announced. Would they keep talking even if Agatha didn’t come to the city?

 

She felt her heart rate pick up, she needed to remember to say her special phrase or she knew there would be no chance of meeting Agatha later. The problem was, she hadn’t exactly planned out when she could say it. She felt the production assistant tap her arm and she nodded, moving through the curtains and under the unforgiving lights.

 

She smiled, feeling out of place the moment she hit the stage. Her eyes tried to adjust as she waved, finding it hard to see the crowd. She took the offered mic and pointed at the back of house staff. “Hey, can we turn the lights down a bit,” She smiled a real smile as her request was granted. “Thank you.” She smirked as it dawned on her, and she found the perfect place to drop her code phrase. “Ah, there you are beautiful people! Te veo!” The crowd erupted into applause and Rio found a camera recording her and threw a wink into its direction, just for good measure.

 

***

 

Agatha sat in her hotel room in Chicago, feeling like a fraud. She could never afford this place on her own, not with the way her divorce was currently panning out. She sat with her bags still packed, ready to bolt. The people downstairs hadn’t given her any trouble, but she felt her cheeks burn with embarrassment anyways. As if everyone knew she hadn’t paid for this, she was being bought. 

 

She sat staring at her phone, refreshing her socials, hoping that someone would post videos of Rio’s panel sometime soon. Her eyes lifted to the room phone and she contemplated ordering alcohol to calm her nerves when she remembered, it wasn’t mystery woman’s card that was on the line for this weekend should she spend more than just the room, it was hers.

 

She jumped as she got a social media message from herself, her mouth finally finding a smile.

 

Agatha H: Hey.

 

She rolled her eyes, how like Nicky to steal her laptop.

 

Agatha Harkness: I thought Grandma didn’t want you on electronics?

 

She could practically hear her son giggle. He was a good boy, but he sure did have a mischievous streak and a thing for toeing the lines when it came to the rules. He was so her son. 

 

Agatha H: she’s asleep.

 

She felt her shoulders loosen, if only a bit. As much as she wanted him to listen, she also loved that when it came to his grandmother’s rules, he would still break them for his mom. 

 

Agatha Harkness: You’re being naughty, Nicky.

 

She was swept up in her love for her son when she remembered one very important detail. One that made her chest seize briefly. 

 

Agatha Harkness: Nicky, you’re grounded if you read my messages. There are adult conversations in there. Only talk to me on here, okay?

 

Agatha felt her palms sweating, she really didn’t need her son having questions about what she and some person named @riovidalswhore69 were discussing. She cringed, nor did she need questions about what that particular name entailed. She blew raspberries into the air. It was too late now. She just needed to pray for divine intervention that he wouldn’t go looking too far into things. 

 

Nicky replied with a side eye emoji. 

 

I’m not snooping. I just missed you and wanted to know if you got there safely. I can go back to watching my show now if you are busy. I only have so long before Grandma wakes up.

 

Agatha shook her head at her son’s attitude. It did warm her heart a bit that he had chosen to speak with her over watching his precious show, he was a little kid after all. 

 

Well, I wouldn’t want you to miss tv time. Call me later?

 

Her eyes lit up at the response. Her stress melted away. 

I will. Love you momma.

 

She felt tears prickle around her eyes, as they always did even after all these years with her son in her life. 

 

Love you too, Nicky.

 

As she exited the chat she got a ping. And then another from Nicky.

 

Who’s RioVidalsWhore69?

 

She literally smacked herself in the face, of course he would see it.

 

A Friend, Nicolas. Don’t snoop, go watch your show.

 

She watched the chat for a tense moment, hoping this was the end of that conversation. When nothing more was said, she breathed a sigh of relief as she opened a different message.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: So I am hoping something gets posted soon. I don’t see anything yet, but I’ve been done for about forty minutes. I’m… really hoping to see you today.

 

Blue eyes darted around the room before she responded, realizing that maybe a small hotel room wasn’t the safest way to meet anyone. She wanted to kick herself for not thinking about that detail a little sooner. She was a mom, she had a son to make it home safe to. 

 

@downyourroad: We should meet in public.

 

Her eyes watching as fake Rio tried to come up with a response.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: That’s going to be a bit challenging when there are hundreds of people around the city that are on the lookout for me today, knowing I’m in town. 

 

Agatha rubbed at her stomach. Even if this woman was somehow who she said she was, the fact was, she didn’t know her. 

 

@downyourroad: I’m a woman alone in a hotel room. I don’t know what kind of idiot you take me for, but I won’t be getting murdered so easily.

 

She stood and walked to the door to make sure she engaged the extra latch. That would at least give her time to call for help if some big dude showed up to try and kidnap her. 

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: look, it’s far easier to get people alone than you think. But if that is a condition… I am sure I can think of something. I was just about to head out actually. Want to grab coffee, maybe? I’ll need it to be decently far from this hotel the convention is at. Do you mind taking a cab?

 

Agatha rolled her shoulders as she typed.

 

@downyourroad: I drove. I can take my car.

 

An eye roll emoji was sent back.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: Sweetheart, then I would know your license plate. I have a decent photographic memory, let’s not tempt me. I texted my friend, she has a cafe in Rogers Park, near a small university. Will that suffice? It’s public, plenty of kids around… might be bad for me, but we’ll see how long I last – you’re worth the risk. I can attempt a disguise if needed.

 

Agatha sighed. Her fingers typing slowly, reading over her words a few times before hitting send. Her mind told her to calm down, there was no way this was the real Rio Vidal, but she was about to meet somebody. 

 

@downyourroad: I told you I don’t have any money. I’ll have to drive.

 

A response was almost immediate.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: I’ll send a car. Be down stairs in ten. And yes, I’ll send you money for your trip back in case we don’t go together.

 

And just about as soon as the message was sent Billy was wiring her two hundred dollars. Agatha’s eyes went wide. This woman had said she didn’t make a lot, but she was sure throwing money at her as if she did.

Chapter 11

Agatha tried to never wear her glasses in public, they were big and she felt like a nerd about to be shoved into a locker with them on, but she wanted her eyesight to be sharp as she watched the people come and go in the café. 

 

Mystery woman had indeed sent her a car to this address. It was quiet and there were bookshelves everywhere with old and new books for sale, as well as an eclectic coffee and tea selection. She pushed her glasses higher up her nose as she watched the door open yet again, her eyes glancing down at her phone, though it hadn’t indicated any activity. She navigated to her messages and there was nothing more from fake Rio. Was she about to be stood up?

 

She had thought about ordering, but she panicked at the last second that that might be rude. She should wait, shouldn’t she? It’s not like she should be buying herself a latte when she could spend that extra eight dollars on Nicky later. She leaned back in her plush chair, her fingers effortlessly finding the window where Rio’s panel video was still up, it had finally posted in the car on her way over. She clicked play to watch it again, jumping as her phone speakers crackled to life. Her fingers moved quickly to silence the video. 

 

She had to hand it to her mystery woman, she was good. Rio had opened this morning by saying “Te veo” nearly one minute into her appearance. She rolled her eyes, there had to be an explanation for this. Her body tensed as some kid in a dark hoodie with large sunglasses sat across from her at her little table. She grumbled.

 

“I’m waiting for someone.” When the person didn’t move, she let her eyes flick up from her phone. A woman with a hood pulled over her dark hair and dark glasses staring back at her, now with a smirk firmly in place.

 

“I’m aware.” Her face seemed to take in Agatha, pointing at her own face. “Cute glasses.”

 

The voice was quiet but Agatha’s eyes widened. Her mouth opened just slightly before it closed, her eyes narrowing. This had to be a trick. “Come again?”

 

The person in front of her, in sweats, shook her head before pushing her hood back and lifting her glasses up onto her head, her dark eyes taking in Agatha’s blue for the first time in person. “I mean… I was trying to be discreet, but if the lady needs me to be more clear,” She took a sip of her drink without breaking eye contact. “Hey, gorgeous.” She winked as she leaned forward. “Sorry I’m late. There’s some stupid convention in town and it was a bit crazy getting out of the city center.”

 

Agatha froze. Her eyes were not grasping what she was seeing. Was she hallucinating?

 

Rio side-eyed her for a moment before her dark gaze drifted to the menu over at the ordering counter. “Did you want something to drink or eat? It’s a little late for brunch, but I think we can make an exception.” Her eyes drifted back.

 

Agatha’s eyes dropped to her lap, her cheeks flaring red. She tucked some fallen hair behind her ear. Her mind tried to block out the encounter as if it were some traumatic event. She jumped when her phone buzzed her eyes looking down at a new message.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: You okay? Did you want a drink or something?

 

Agatha’s eyes lifted to Rio, the woman looking down intently at her phone, continuing to type.

 

@RioVidalsWhore69: Alice says that the cinnamon drink tastes like Christmas, but I’ve yet to try it. Do you like sweet? My drink is vanilla and loaded with sugar… you can try it if you want?

 

Agatha felt like she might faint. She heard Rio move but didn’t register that she had left, until she came back with a bag of ice, gently taking Agatha’s wrist and placing the plastic baggie covered in brown paper towel over her veins.

 

“This should help,” Her voice was soft, her eyes trained on Agatha’s skin, a private smirk lighting up her whole face. “I knew your skin would be soft.” Her eyes remained low, allowing Agatha to take her in.

 

Blue eyes darted down to the ice and Rio’s hand on her as she swallowed and tried to speak. “What… what are you doing?”

 

Rio repositioned the ice and shrugged. “This is one way to fight a panic attack.” Her eyes lifted. “I don’t think drugging you would be a good way to calm you down. We’ve only just met, and I know how concerned you are about strangers.”

 

Agatha closed her mouth and nodded. Her eyes flitted around the room. “T-Thank you.”

 

Rio nodded. “So, drink?” She took Agatha’s other hand and placed it over the bag of ice. “Just keep that on a few more minutes, until your nerves balance out.”

 

Agatha’s eyes looked at the menu, speaking as if on autopilot. “I like cinnamon.” She kept her eyes far from Rio’s, the ice helping her stay present. 

 

Rio nodded and bounded over to the barista to place the order. The woman’s eyes widening as they took her in. Rio leaned on the counter and flirted a bit before she walked away with another cup. She set it down gently in front of Agatha. “My lady.”

 

Agatha let out a breath. “Thank you.”

 

Rio nodded. “So… you’re a bit… quiet in person.” She sipped more of her drink as she tilted her head. “Not what I expected from the things you said to me… nor sent me.”

 

Agatha’s bit her lip, flushing. Wanting to die on the spot. “I… I’m a bit unfiltered online.”

 

Rio nodded, her smile intrigued. “Oh, I know.”

 

Agatha took her cup and sipped the drink for something to occupy her hands with, her eyes flashing as the drink really was good.

 

Agatha set the bag of ice on the table before tapping her fingers nervously on her thigh, one finger at a time in quick succession. “So…  you–you wanted to meet me?”

 

Rio flicked her long side bangs from her eyes. “Yeah,” she smirked. “I did.”
