CHAPTER 20

Agatha stepped out of the back of her taxi with her son. Her eyes staring up at a gated home she didn’t know. Her stomach was in knots. This had been the address Rio had given her. It was in the hills, though Rio insisted that its location near the bottom meant that it wasn’t anything to be impressed with. Agatha let out a puff of air. This house easily cost at least a few million. She tried to settle her feelings but found that she was going to be sick if she so much as breathed too much.

 

Nicky grabbed his bag and nudged his mother, her eyes finally drifting down to him, his smile bright as he took her hand. “She has a dog!” He pulled his mother and suitcase along as Agatha snatched up her bags with her other hand.

 

Agatha had been quiet since her breakdown. She found that her hand shook as she reached to call Rio, Nicky taking over without a fuss. Her eyes burned with embarrassment. Maybe once she was able to settle in, she would feel more normal. Her hand rubbed at her chest, relying on another person wasn’t something she was used to, nor did it normally go well, but Rio had said this was temporary. She was just helping her get on her feet. She closed her eyes and prayed to her patron goddess that this was about to go well. When she saw Rio come walking out the front door with a shy smile on her face.

 

“Hey you two!” She opened the gate and Nicky wrapped his arms around her looking up with a smile.

 

“Hey, Rio.” She ran her hand through his hair and stuck out her tongue. The boy repeated the motion back before giggling. Agatha stood quietly by, watching the interaction with intrigue. Her son wasn’t normally so open with others. She watched as Nicky moved to help himself into the house and Rio turned to let her eyes connect with Agatha’s. “Can I help you with that?”

 

Agatha’s mouth opened but before she could protest, Rio took the handle and threw the duffle over her shoulder. “How was your flight?”

 

The other woman walked quickly behind her. “It was fine. I…slept.” 

 

Rio inclined her head as she led them inside, finding Nicky on the floor petting Ruffland. Rio nodded at her son. “Ruffland.” She whistled and the dog looked up panting, Rio pointed. “This is Agatha,” then she pointed at Nicky. “And you met Nicky.”

 

She took their bags, “I’ll put these in your rooms.” Agatha looked at Nicky with the dog and upon her analysis that the dog wouldn’t eat her child, she took off her shoes and quickly followed Rio down the hall. “Rooms?”

 

Rio kept moving, “Yeah, I figured you and Nicky needed your own space. It’s just down the hall,” Her head indicating some stairs up ahead. “My room is up there.”

Agatha placed her fingers to her lips then raised them to reach out when Rio opened her door and set her bag and duffle inside. “I didn’t have much time to prepare the space, but I hope it’s okay.” Her eyes turned to Agatha while her hands found her back pockets. “It’s got a bathroom.” She looked around, “Did you want me to set up your laptop on the desk?”

 

Agatha shook her head. “I can do that…” She watched as Rio ducked out of the room past her, moving Nicky’s bag to the next room down the hall. Between Agatha’s room and another downstairs bathroom. “Nicky’s room is right here, I grabbed a couple of things, I didn’t know what he would like. We can still take him to the store later…”

 

Agatha peaked into the room and rubbed at her neck. “Rio… when you said you didn’t have money…”

 

Rio sighed. “I don’t… in comparison to my peers. I can’t,” She let her eyes widen for a moment, “Like go crazy or anything. I have to watch my budget.”

 

Agatha moved her long hair behind an ear. “I’ll pay you back once I find work.”

 

Rio closed her eyes. “Agatha, I’m fine. None of this has been outside my spending limit. Trust me.”

 

Rio lifted her arm to lean on the doorway. “I can’t like… afford a bigger place than this. I put most of what I make into investments and I try to live off of that.” She shrugged. “I just can’t jet off on vacations and wear only designer brands. I didn’t…” she shrugged, looking at the floor. “Want you thinking that I could give you whatever your heart desired… cause I have totally dated that girl.” She scooted past Agatha. “I’ll get started on lunch, are pizza rolls okay?”

 

Agatha leaned back against the wall. “Yeah… that sounds great.” As Rio left her on her own, she moved into the room and sat down on the bed. The sheets were soft, the comforter cozy. She decided she would just lay down for a moment, when she fell into a dreamless sleep.

 

***

 

It was dark when Nicky woke her up, his little lips kissing her on the temple. “Goodnight, Momma. I’m going to go to bed.”

 

She looked around confused but nodded. “Goodnight, Nicky.” As he left, she pushed herself up, the room feeling slightly less foreign than earlier. She opened her suitcase and grabbed a pair of sweatpants and a cotton shirt. Hopeful that a shower would help her feel more at ease. She wandered into the bathroom and found that the towels were all purple, her eyebrows rising at the detail before discovering that Rio had stocked the bathroom with essentials. She turned on the water and hopped in, taking in the scents that had her mind jumping back to her night with Rio. Her stomach tightening. Her eyes closed as the only sounds in the bathroom became her breathing. She let her hand start at her neck and slide down to her chest. Her body coming back online.

 

She groaned as she grabbed at her own breast. Her mind had clocked Rio’s couch as she walked in, the same couch the woman had imagined Agatha bending her over on. She mewled. She wanted to do that, but she also wanted someone to take control of her right now. Her life felt so out of control since her wife kicked her and Nicky out. She just wanted someone to make sure she didn’t fall any further.

 

She let her hand drift down her stomach when she heard a sound in her room, her door opening. She felt her heart rate speed up further. Rio was looking for her. She turned to the shampoo and quickly moved to clean her hair. She knew she had had a long travel day and she didn’t need Rio seeing her like this. She moved quickly even as her crotch was throbbing in need. She moved to soap herself, finding a fresh razor she cleaned up her body. She rinsed off and conditioned her hair. Wondering where Rio had gone to, or if she was waiting in her room.

 

She moved to turn the water off as she wrapped herself up in a fluffy towel. Her hair still dripping as she moved to peek out of the bathroom, her room was undisturbed. She closed the door and started to dry off, quickly locating some hair lotion then wrapping her hair back in a towel. She moved to set her suitcase on the floor as she found clothing. She pulled out her lace thong and left herself braless as she pulled on her t-shirt and her sweats. This would have to do. She toweled off her hair until it was mostly dry, then she went in search of Rio, needing a distraction.

 

***

 

Rio sat in her bed reading on her phone, a new story had just dropped. Did Agatha still wish for her to write her one? Because she could…

 

She heard her door open as she saw Agatha slip into her room, a smile on her face. Rio set her phone aside. “How did you sleep?”

 

Agatha shrugged. “I would assume well if I was out for hours.”

 

Rio moved closer to the end of the bed. “Did you wanna… talk?”

 

Agatha shook her head. She leaned down and grabbed Rio’s face with both hands, capturing her lips. Rio gasped as she let herself be kissed for a moment before she pulled back. “Agatha… you ended things.”

 

Blue eyes rolled. “And now I’m in your house…”

 

Rio shrugged. “We can be friends.” Brown eyes settled on the bed as her fingers played with the sheets.

 

Agatha sat down searching her face, taken aback. “You’re over me? Just like that?”

 

Rio bit her lip as she tried to tame her smile at the insinuation. “I’m not over you…”

 

Agatha seemed to like that answer as she moved to straddle her lap, as Rio leaned back on her hands. “Agatha…”

 

The woman on top of her lifted a hand to cup her jaw, a thumb brushing over Rio’s lips. “I don’t want to think tonight.” 

 

Rio raised a hand and ran it up and down Agatha’s side. “Okay…”

 

The woman leaned forward and captured her lips again, and as she ground into Rio’s lap the dark haired beauty let out a quiet moan. 

 

Agatha smiled into her lips, relieved. “So you did miss me.”

 

Rio’s eyes were lidded as she nodded at her, her mind rushing with feelings. Feelings Agatha didn’t want to deal with, she knew that, so she kept her mouth shut and kissed her. Her lover quickly noticed that she was distracted. 

 

“What do you need, Rio?” Agatha said. 

 

Rio blinked her eyes rapidly as she shook her head. “I’m just glad you and Nicky are okay.” She swallowed. “I’m open to whatever you need right now.”

 

Agatha sat back, moving off of Rio’s lap. “You don’t want sex?” 

 

Rio shrugged. “I’m down if that’s what you need, but we could also just… relax. Or… cuddle.” She bit her lip. 

 

Agatha snorted, crossing her arms. “I don’t cuddle.” 

 

Rio smirked. “Well, I know that’s not true.”

 

Agatha leaned back and Rio grabbed her wrist. “Don’t go… please.”

 

The woman froze then settled. 

 

Rio’s eyes were wet. “The couch is just in the other room you know,” She tried to lighten the mood but wasn’t successful, “but I don’t think we should do that while Nicky’s home.” She tried to smile at her joke and her hand quickly lifted to wipe away her own tears, though the brunette had seen them.

 

Agatha’s eyes watched her with sadness. “You…”

 

Rio shook her head. “You scared me, alright?”

 

Agatha sat there watching Rio for a few moments before she pulled her lover to her. Rio’s face pressing firmly into her shoulder. Agatha was never great at words, so she just held Rio, finding that maybe she needed this too. Her mind settled as she was pulled down to the bed. The other woman was laying her head on her chest. Agatha’s hand came up to play with her hair as she stared at the ceiling, long after Rio had begun to snore.

CHAPTER 21 

 

Rio opened her eyes, feeling around for Agatha. Upon noticing that the space beside her had gone cold, she wondered if Agatha and Nicky were even there with her or if all of that were some weird dream. Her eyes glanced at her partially opened bedroom door. Ruffland never let her sleep in this late. She stood and grabbed a hoodie, padding down the hall towards the kitchen, soft sounds starting to come into focus.

 

“Hey, Momma, do you think Rio would let me play with Ruffland in the yard?”

 

Rio’s eyes landed on Agatha, who was cooking at the stove. It wasn’t like she minded, though she did wish she would have been around to be a part of the morning routine. She wouldn’t have minded helping.

 

Agatha addressed Nicky. “You’ll have to wait until she’s awake to ask her. Did you find the dog's food?”

 

Nicky nodded. “The food in the fridge had his name on it. I wasn’t sure how much to give him so I only gave him a little.”

 

Rio cleared her throat and all eyes in the room fell to her. “Morning.” She smiled as Ruffland came over and licked her hand. Her eyes crinkling at the affection. “Hey baby, did someone feed you this morning?” 

 

Nicky came over and bounced on his toes. “Is Ruffland allowed to play ball in the backyard?”

 

Rio smiled. She had a feeling her dog had found his new best friend. “Yes, did you two want to go play?” He nodded and took off for the back door, the dog hot on his heels. Rio crossed her arms and raised an eyebrow at the woman at the stove. “I could have made us something.”

 

Agatha turned back to what she was cooking, trying to keep busy. “I figured I could help, especially with you letting us stay here.” 

 

Rio moved to her side and rubbed at her back, noticing how Agatha twitched. Rio took her hand away and cleared her throat. “Sorry, I ruined the mood last night.”

 

Agatha shrugged. “It’s fine. You had a rough night.” She continued moving food around. 

 

Rio bit her lip, she hoped she wasn’t messing things up already. “I think it was you who was having a rough night.” She moved to get the juice from the fridge, wondering desperately if there was more she could be doing to help the Harkness family feel at home. “Is there anything else you and Nicky need?”

 

Agatha’s shoulders dropped, her voice going quiet. “You’ve done enough.”

 

Rio let her hair fall forward, leaning against the counter. Her shoulders shrugging. “I don’t mind.”

 

Agatha moved the plate of eggs off of the burner next to the pancakes. “I’m not used to… kindness.” She wrung her hands as she avoided Rio’s gaze. “I’m trying to understand.”

 

Rio moved to get the plates and fix the kitchen table, making herself useful. “I didn’t always have the easiest life.”

 

Agatha crossed her arms a thought hitting her. “I must admit, you are pretty stingy on personal details in interviews.” Blue eyes studying the dark haired beauty at the table. 

 

Rio rolled her eyes, wiggling her fingers at Agatha. “I cast my spell, people laugh, everyone’s happy. And no one knows too much about me.” She took a deep breath, letting it out slowly as her eyes moved back to plates. “I like it that way.”

 

Agatha moved the rest of the food to the table. “I can understand that. I don’t like to talk to people about my life either. Too many opinions if you talk to other people.”

 

Rio leaned up and kissed Agatha on the corner of the mouth, the woman turning slightly to chase the feeling before Rio smirked and moved away. So she did want some physical affection, Rio took notes. “I’ll go get Nicky.” She ran her hand down Agatha’s arm as she disappeared to get the boys.

 

***

 

Agatha sat down feeling off center. Rio let Nicky pick where he wanted to sit, then gave Ruffland a bit of a snack. Breakfast was decently quiet, Nicky and Rio had an in depth conversation about bugs in California, as Agatha zoned out. 

 

Rio noticed her phone flashing out of the corner of her eye and raised a hand indicating she would just be a moment. 

 

“Lilia, hey, what’s up…” she started to leave the room when she paused in the doorway. “She’s here, actually.” Her eyes returned to the woman at the table. She walked quickly back, putting the phone on the table on speakerphone.

 

“Agatha?”

 

Blue eyes flashed at hearing her name. “He-llo?” She fought to quickly swallow the food that was in her mouth, trying not to choke. 

 

The woman over the phone came through again. “It’s Lilia, Rio’s agent. How are you, dear?”

 

She ran her hand through her dark brown hair. “I’m… I’m good. How… how are you?”

 

Lilia dove right in. “We need to discuss some details about your audition. Do you have an agent, dear?”

 

Agatha’s eyes lifted to Rio who was talking quietly with Nicky, trying not to listen. Agatha shook her head. “No… Ma’am. I sort of… haven’t found anyone yet. Rio only suggested I start reading for things recently.”

 

Lilia tutted. “Well, this role is a very big deal, Miss Harkness. Rio has been working very hard to land an opportunity like this one. Perhaps we should speak in private.” Rio raised an eyebrow but Agatha didn’t look her way instead, she stood on unsteady legs and took the woman off speaker as she wandered into the tv room. “I understand. I have… moved to a different room.”

 

“Miss Harkness, since you are starting out, my fees are higher than they are for Rio. She’s been a client for a very long time, but on her word that you possess a great talent, I would like to represent you.”

Agatha’s hands shook. “That, that would be great. Thank… thank you very much.”

 

Lilia snorted. “Rio, is a dear friend of mine. Don’t hurt her.”

 

Agatha felt sick. “I… I won’t.”

 

Lilia tutted. “Good. This role, should you book it, is directly opposite her. As you can imagine, if you book this, a lot is about to change. Everyone wants to be famous, Miss Harkness, no one understands what that actually means until they are in it. Before we continue, you won't be able to live life as if you are invisible anymore. Someone will recognize you no matter where you go, your son will be recognizable, despite our best efforts. Your association with Rio will be speculated by some and ignored by others. Speaking of, what are your intentions with Miss Vidal?”

 

Agatha felt like she was meeting Rio’s mother all of a sudden, the realization crashing all around her like treacherous waves in a storm. “I… I don’t know.”

 

Lilia’s voice hardened. “Don’t lead her on, Miss Harkness. If you don’t love her. Keep it moving, keep it professional.”

 

Agatha remained quiet as Lilia spoke again. “I have a meeting with Sharon tomorrow. I will hopefully know something about their decision on your involvement. If it’s a no, I have two other projects I would like you to read for, but I want to keep you available for this one first.”

 

Agatha almost asked who “Sharon” was, but held her tongue. “Yes, Ma’am.”

 

Lilia started typing. “Good talk. I need to go. Tell Rio I said I will see her tomorrow.”

 

Agatha nodded. “I will.”

 

Lilia sighed. “How long will you be staying with her?”

 

Agatha stalled, but before she could find an answer, Lilia excused herself. 

 

“Oh hell, what is Taryn doing? I gotta go. Talk tomorrow.” The line went dead.

Chapter 22

Chapter Summary

Agatha and Rio try and acclimate to each other and Rio tries to spend time with Agatha.

Congrats to Sarah P who won the next chapter dropping today :) Thank you all for the reviews on the last chapter i was honestly surprised that chapter got so much love.

Chapter 22 

Agatha had been in her head the rest of the day. She had cleaned up the kitchen then retreated to her room. Rio and Nicky had asked if she wanted to watch a movie with them, but she declined, saying she didn’t feel well, that she had a headache. 

 

She received a text soon after, a photo showing her that Rio had left her painkillers and fluids outside her door. She rolled her eyes as she retrieved them. Settling in bed, she grabbed her laptop and pulled up a search for apartments, the amounts on even the studios were quite a bit outside of her assumed range. She wished she had asked Lilia how much the role paid, but figured it didn’t matter as long as it was something better than she was making before.

 

She cuddled under her blankets and quickly nodded off again. She sighed upon waking, realizing that she had never felt this tired before in her life. She wondered if it was because for once, she felt she could breathe and let her guard down to sleep. She blew her hair from her face as she checked her phone. A photo of food in the fridge, for her, warmed her heart. Rio had taken care of Nicky again. She bit her lip. She wasn’t hungry. Not yet, but she started to text Rio, cringing at the time. How had she slept that late?

 

Thank you for making dinner. I’m… sorry I slept the day away… again.

 

Rio: It’s alright. Nicky helped me cook. Then he took a shower and went to watch a movie in his room. I checked on him a while ago and he’s knocked out. You two deserve some good rest.

 

Agatha settled back into the bed wishing she knew what to write to keep the conversation going.

 

***

 

Rio got ready for bed and saw her phone flash. Agatha was writing to her again. She sighed when she noticed the woman was wanting to make an effort to engage but wasn’t sure how. She glanced toward her bedroom door before she responded.

 

Did you want me to come keep you company? Rio asked. 

 

Agatha stopped writing and Rio let her head fall back slightly. She didn’t know what the right answers were when it came to Agatha. She locked her phone and decided to make some tea, then seek her out.

 

She knocked on Agatha’s door not long after the kettle had boiled enough for tea. When the woman didn’t appear, she tried the door knob, it opened. She ducked her head in and saw Agatha leaning up against the headboard watching her phone intently. 

 

Rio took a step inside and noticed Agatha jump at the sound. “I made you something to drink.” She offered. 

 

Blue eyes looked about trying to make room for her, scooting over slightly. Rio smirking at the attempt, before going to hand Agatha her drink. 

 

“Did you want company?”

 

Agatha shrugged. “You’re already here. I’m not going to tell you what to do in your own home.”

 

Rio rolled her eyes as she slid in next to Agatha, the woman tensing as Rio looked at her phone. Her eyes took in a very different version of Agatha. “Is that when you were carrying Nicky?”

 

Agatha took in a shaky breath. “Yeah… I looked…”

 

Rio leaned her shoulder into Agatha’s. “Cute.”

 

Agatha gaped at her. “Cute? Ew. No.”

 

Rio giggled. “I’m pretty sure you looked normal, I hear people have to accommodate a living being in their body to have a baby.”

 

Agatha glared at Rio as the raven haired woman lifted her hands in surrender. “Hey, it’s not an interest of mine, but…” she took a sip of her drink, shrugging. “Your kid’s cute.” Her eyes flashed in panic. “Not that I want one.”

 

Agatha snorted. “Ah, so you haven’t been trying to knock me up? Could have fooled me.”

 

Rio smiled. “No.” Her eyes drifted back to the phone, taking it and flipping through the photos, even though Agatha pouted.

 

“How was it, carrying Nicky?”

 

Agatha leaned her head back on the headboard, her shoulders collapsing. “Painful.”

 

Rio’s eyes lingered on the phone. “Well, I hear that’s normal, too. At least you got what you wanted in the end.”

 

Agatha looked around carefully before she whispered her admission. “I… didn’t want children.”

 

Rio’s eyes turned to her, her lips turning downward. “Then why…”

 

Agatha clasped her hands in front of her before studying her fingers. “Tori… did.”

 

Rio’s hand reached for Agatha’s. “Then why did you,”

 

Agatha tried to swallow her tears. “Isn’t that what you do when you love someone?”

 

Rio’s eyes drifted back to the phone, her heart stopping. More pieces of the woman before her clicked into place in her mind. Her voice was soft as she reached out. “No, Agatha. That’s not the only way to love someone.”

 

Agatha’s finger flipped to a different photo, trying to distract from her darker feelings. Deep down she knew Tori’s love was wrong, that things weren’t right. She never felt great, but she had thought that was just love. That she needed to just live with it, because someone had finally taken an interest in her. And Tori had been beautiful and powerful, and she had loved Tori so much that she was willing to hurt herself to prove it. 

 

She pointed at the next photo hoping to distract Rio, “I was huge.”

 

Rio snorted. “I stand by what I said. You’re still adorable.”

 

Agatha cringed. “The hormone injections really got to me.”

 

Dark eyes continued to study the images, realizing that Agatha didn’t seem happy. “IVF?”

 

Agatha nodded. “Yep. Tori wasn’t… happy that I struggled to have Nicky. We really pushed the limits on what my body could handle.”

 

Rio tapped on Agatha’s thigh, trying to take it all in. Her own admission slipping past her lips. “So, I don’t… like kids.”

 

Agatha’s eyes widened. “I… I’m sorry. Nicky can stay in his room… I’ll make sure his things are always put away.” She threw off the covers to make sure that Nicky’s things were out of sight, when Rio caught her. 

 

“Agatha. Stop. That’s not what I meant. I… I like Nicky.” She held her gaze, “A lot. He’s different.”

 

Agatha’s eyes were wary. “Children are a lot, and I don’t want to burden you.” She finished off leaving plenty unsaid. 

 

Rio shook her head. “Let me try that again. I like your child.” She handed Agatha her phone back. “He reminds me of you.”

 

Agatha let her eyes fall to the bed. “You’re…very good with him.” She bit her cheek. “Makes me jealous sometimes.”

 

Rio shrugged. “I’m just new, and a big kid at heart. I’m just his friend.”

 

Agatha rubbed at her arms. “I’m sorry we invaded your life. I promise we won’t stay long…”

 

Rio crossed her legs and leaned back on her hands. “Don’t do that. I was going to ask you to come anyway. Both of you, I just… got nervous.” She shrugged when Agatha’s eyes grew wider. “You thought I was already overstepping when I met him. I was worried you would stop speaking to me altogether if I suggested you move here.”

 

Agatha rubbed at her face. “It isn’t the easiest thing to do.” She closed her eyes as she felt Rio’s hands weave into her hair. Her voice fading as she was taken over by the feeling. “I’m sure I’ll get used to the idea.” She moaned as Rio started to scratch at her scalp.

 

“You’re a good mom, Agatha. Nicky is lucky to have you.” She continued her movements as she took in Agatha up close, the lines of her jaw, the soft and long lashes at her eyes, the way she tried to swallow down her emotions. How she wished she could see her crystal blue eyes right now, but she wasn’t about to take away Agatha’s comfort, not so she could have what she wanted. 

 

Rio’s eyes tried to memorize everything about Agatha, from her hair color, the multiple dimensions to it, to her skin tone, to the lines on her skin – which had lessened since she had gotten more sleep. Her heart clenched, as visions of a future she desperately wanted came uninvited. Her mind making sure the connection to her mouth was severed, she didn’t need to be scaring this woman off the moment she got there. 

 

Agatha opened her eyes and caught Rio staring, her cheeks flushing. “Stop looking at me like that.”

 

Rio’s eyes settled on Agatha’s bright blue. “Like what?”

 

She felt as Agatha’s eyes pierced into her soul. “Like you want me here.”

 

Rio affirmed her worst fears. “I do want you here.”

CHAPTER 23 - Congrats

 

Rio stretched and felt around the bed. The sheets felt slightly different than she was used to. Her messy bed-head popped up to take in her environment. One of her guest bedrooms… No. It wasn’t anymore, it was Agatha’s room now. Her eyes froze on Agatha’s back sitting at the desk bathed in sunlight. Hunched over her head resting in one hand as she drew with a pencil in the other.

 

Rio tried not to breathe her eyes watching in awe as Agatha created in her drawing book. She noticed how Agatha tensed.

 

“You stopped snoring.” Agatha whispered. 

 

Rio’s face lit up amused. “I don’t snore.”

 

Agatha laughed quietly. “You do.” Her eyes didn’t leave her work.

 

Rio figured since Agatha already knew she was awake, she could push her luck and try and get closer. She crawled across the bed on her hands and knees, before shifting her legs off the bed to stand. She walked the couple feet to Agatha and wrapped her arms lightly over her shoulders. Her eyes taking in the artwork, her breath unsteady.

 

“Woah.”

 

Agatha continued to draw though her body relaxed under Rio’s warmth. 

 

“Agatha, that’s amazing.” She fought the urge to touch the image. “You really made my eyes look… alive.”

 

The woman continued to trace the graphite around the paper. “Your eyes are prettier.”

 

Rio leaned her chin on Agatha’s shoulder. She didn’t see how that could be possible. “ Your eyes are prettier.” She pulled Agatha’s hair away from her neck as she added a kiss to her sensitive skin, feeling her twitch slightly.

 

Rio looked back at the image. “Which of my characters is she?”

 

Agatha's hand drifted down to her drawing’s neckline, no outfit revealing that detail yet. Her lips hesitated before she let the truth out on a whispered breath. “You.”

 

Rio moved to kiss her cheek. Agatha shifting away. “She’s not done yet.”

 

The younger woman squeezed her shoulder as she moved. “Well, I can’t wait to see when she is.”

 

She left Agatha to her creative solitude as she readied herself for the day back in her bathroom. Nicky found her quickly enough. “Hey, Rio?” She lightly jumped at the sound, her hand pressing on her chest to still her heart. 

 

“Yeah?”

 

He shuffled his feet, “Sorry.”

 

Rio turned around leaning on her vanity. “Don’t sweat it, I’m cool. What did you want to talk about?”

 

He chewed at his lip before he spoke. “Your phone has been ringing. I was going to tell you sooner… but you and Momma were… cuddling.”

 

Rio’s eyes went wide. “Oh. Thank you, Nicky. I’ll check it in just a moment.”

 

He nodded as he bounded off. A moment later she heard Ruffland play growling, he must have tricked Nicky into a round of tug-o-war. She shook her head, her dog was a master manipulator. She finished what she was doing and wandered to the kitchen, where the boys were playing as she picked up her phone, her hand covering her mouth quickly.

 

“Oh my god.” She saw the moment Nicky turned, concerned.

 

“What happened?”

 

Rio lowered her hand. “Nicky… you can’t say a word to your mother.”

 

The little boy held her gaze. “I can keep a secret.”

 

Rio motioned for him to come to her as her eyes watched the hall. “Okay, so this is like a very big deal for your mom.”

 

Nicky nodded, looking at the phone and seeing too many words. “Okay. Did she get the job?”

 

Rio nodded excitedly. “She did!” she squealed quietly. “We should… find a special way to tell her.”

 

Nicky nodded, placing his finger to his chin in thought, before he raised it. “A cake.”

 

Rio stood then shrugged. “That’s as good of an idea as any. We should run to the store.”

 

As she was about to tell Nicky to grab his coat, Agatha came wandering in, her steps quiet. “What is everyone doing in here?”

 

Rio’s lips pursed as she tried to think up a lie, while Nicky excitedly started to bounce. “Rio said we can get stuff to make a cake!” He ran up to his mom and threw his arms around her. Her bright blue eyes went even bluer, unless Rio was hallucinating. 

 

“Oh she did, did she?” Her eyes turned to Rio’s. “What’s the occasion?”

 

Rio shrugged, keeping her face clear of emotion. “Kid said he liked cake.” She pointed towards the front room. “If you’re coming, you better get your coat.” The little boy bounded off. Rio adjusted her hair. “Figured you could use the peace and quiet to keep drawing while we did the boring stuff at the store.”

 

Agatha’s eyes fell. Her hand moving her hair behind her ear. “That’s nice of you.” Her fingers playing with her lip. “I was… going to take a break.”

 

Rio watched as Agatha faltered. “Did you, want to come?”

 

Agatha’s eyes lifted. “I mean… if you two wouldn’t mind? I was… getting lonely. I have spent quite a bit of time sleeping.” Her pointer finger indicating her room down the hall. 

 

Rio readjusted Agatha’s hair behind her ear as it had fallen, blue eyes looking up at her. “Totally cool.”

 

Agatha’s hands landed on Rio’s hips but quickly slipped away the moment Nicky came thundering back. Her eyes closed, “Nicky, walk.”

 

The boy slowed immediately as he heard her tone. “Sorry, Momma. Sorry, Rio.”

 

Rio turned Agatha around. “You need to go grab your coat too.”

 

Blue eyes rolled. “It’s like sixty degrees out, I’m practically melting as it is.”

 

Rio snorting at the Midwesterners in her kitchen. “Okay, well I am putting a coat on, at least grab one of my hoodies from my dresser, I promise it will be chilly out.”

 

Agatha disappeared down the hall as Rio moved to the coat closet, taking out a dark green puffer jacket. Her eyes glanced up to thank whatever gods or goddesses were listening for her little comment, because the sight of Agatha in her black hoodie was the cutest thing she had ever seen. She kept her thoughts to herself as they got in the car and ventured to the store. 

 

She noticed Agatha felt out of palace as they shopped, Nicky and Rio trying hard to get her input on the cake. Blue eyes trying to remain passive but Rio could tell something was bothering her. Did it have to do with their conversation last night?

 

Rio’s dark eyes clocked a flower and gift shop as they drove home. She texted Billy that she needed him to pick up a few things. Some flowers as well as place an order for a watch she had seen recently that had been totally Agatha, and in her favorite purple. She would try and swing by and pick both up from him later, that was unless he had time for a delivery. 

 

Rio and Nicky set to work in the kitchen, shooing Agatha away as they started to bake. The woman looked a bit hurt as she stood in the doorway for a while before heading off.

 

Rio and Nicky created an array of different purples for the layers, infusing sprinkles of blue moons and stars everywhere they went, both getting very messy in the process. The icing was a bit runny but they made it work. Finally drawing vines and roots all over the cake. Nicky bit his tongue as he focused, endearing him even more to Rio.

 

When they were done, they high fived and Rio found some paper for them to make a card, setting Nicky loose at her desk in her room while she cleaned up the kitchen and waited for Billy. Her eyes glued to her phone.

 

She felt her before she heard her, her lover hovering by the kitchen entryway. “Rio?”

 

The girl didn’t look up as she gave some small vocal indication that she had heard her. Her eyes finally saw the note from Billy that he was almost there.

 

“Did I do something wrong?”

 

Rio’s eyes shot up as Agatha’s voice trembled. “Because…”

 

Rio shook her head. “Stop, what has gotten into you?”

 

Agatha shook her head. “Maybe it’s the hormones…” She took a step back. “Menopause.” she shrugged. She rubbed at her stomach. “I just can’t shake the feeling that…” her words faded as the doorbell rang. Her eyes chasing the sound. “Were you expecting someone?”

 

Rio moved forward and patted her arm in passing, “Stay here, we’re not done with this conversation.”

 

Rio opened the door and chipper little gay boy Billy stood bouncing on the balls of his feet. “Morning, Rio!” After a quick glance at his watch he shook his head laughing. “Or afternoon! So I picked it all up, then… I added something a little extra.” He grinned. “This little bunny plush was just so cute I couldn’t stand it.”

 

Rio smirked. Well, she hopped Agatha like rabbits. “Sweet, Billy, Thanks for doing that.”

 

He handed it over carefully, “No problem! So the flowers are exactly what you asked for, minus, the one I had to swap out because you totally asked for a flower that meant death.”

 

Rio cringed. “Ah, again?” 

 

Billy nodded. “Yeah, not very, congratulations my love. More like, I’d like to see you six feet under, horizontal, in a grave.”

 

Rio snorted. “Fair enough.” She let her nose sniff the bouquet as she set the present bag down that presumably held the watch and bunny. She sighed. “This is wonderful, good teamwork.”

 

She leaned on the doorway. “So… where is boyf today?”

 

BIlly blushed, “Across town in studio city, at dance rehearsals.”

 

Rio winked. “Eddie is a lucky guy, I hope he’s working hard. You guys have any plans this weekend?”

 

Billy rubbed the back of his neck. “Yeah, we’re going to check out that Ocean Club in Santa Monica, the back room with your connection.” He tried to suppress his grin. “Just like… try not to need me tonight?”

 

Rio crossed her heart. “You got it. I’ll make myself scarce.”

 

Billy looked up when he saw the woman he had Venmoed enter the hall. He gave a little wave. “Ah, so you did get her to yourself after all?” He winked. “Classic, Rio.”

 

She rolled her dark eyes before pushing at his shoulder. “Get out of here, I’ll introduce you another time.” He saluted her as he skipped to his car. Rio shook her head and closed the door.

 

Agatha’s chin was raised as she avoided her eyes. “And who is he ?” Her voice ticked up at the end, in thinly veiled alarm.

 

Rio hid the flowers behind her back and scooted the present under the entrance table. “No one.” Her face was tense. “Go back to the other room.”

 

Agatha looked her up and down before she spun on the balls of her feet, bypassing the kitchen and heading for her room.

 

Rio’s mouth dropped open as she set the flowers down on the table. “Agatha!”

 

The woman didn’t slow down and Rio watched as she moved her hand to wipe at her face. 


“Agatha, would you stop!” Rio’s voice was frustrated. “It’s just Billy.”

 

Agatha turned with her eyes narrowed. “Just, Billy?”

 

Rio stopped where she was as she felt that Agatha would launch at her if she came any closer. “Yeah… my assistant?” She pointed at Agatha. “The same kid that wired money to you, for me?”

 

Agatha crossed her arms. “How nice for him. Is he even legal?”

 

Rio raised her eyebrows as if Agatha had gone insane. “What?”

 

The woman gripped herself tighter. Rio raising a hand. “Okay, I don’t know what that was but…”

 

Agatha started to tap her foot. “You’re hiding things.” She pressed her fingers to her forehead. “He brought you flowers…”

 

Rio took a step towards Agatha, her hands held out in surrender. “Yes, as I asked him to.”

 

Agatha tensed as Rio moved closer still. “Why would you ask him to?”

 

Rio let her fingers lightly wrap around Agatha’s arm when she got close enough. “Me and Nicky have a surprise for you. Can you… just give me a chance to show you before you bite my head off about my affections for my very gay assistant?”

 

Agatha deflated. “He’s gay?”

 

Rio snorted. “Could you not see his eyeliner from down the hall? He’s wearing pink eyeshadow today too.” She deadpanned. “Just my type, a fairy twink.”

 

Agatha rolled her eyes. “I just thought…”

 

Rio leaned forward into her space and cupped her cheek. “Stop thinking.” Agatha huffed and Rio eased the other woman’s arms from around herself. She lifted her voice and called out for Nicky who yelled back from down the hall.

 

“Almost, ready!”

 

Agatha’s fingers came to her mouth as she started to bite at her nails, but Rio intercepted them before she could cause damage. “Come with me.” She took her back down the hall and placed her at the kitchen table. Leaving her there as her and Nicky gathered the items. Moving to place them on the table in front of Agatha, as blue eyes looked on in horror. Rio was not accustomed to her emotions, but if her son’s reactions were anything to go by, then it seemed Agatha would be alright momentarily.



Agatha settled her hands in her lap as she looked expectantly at the two people before her, waiting. Nicky looked to Rio and with a nod he handed the card to his mom, before he grunted taking it back quickly and shoving a pen into Rio’s hands, she quickly understood and signed it before handing it back to him. He then shoved it back into his mother’s outstretching fingers.

 

“There. Read it.”

 

***

 

Agatha couldn’t breathe, why had they done this for her? She opened the card and her eyes scanned the words not quite understanding. Congratulations? For what? Her eyes lifted to her son and Rio, shrugging. “What is this for?”

 

Rio patted Nicky on the back and he blurted out. “You got the job, Momma!”

 

She froze, her eyes blinking steadily. “What…” Her gaze lifted to Rio’s. “What does he mean?”

 

Rio squatted before her, taking her hand. “I got an email from Lilia this morning, asking if I wanted to tell you the news. So… welcome to The Forest with me, Agatha!” 

 

Agatha stood immediately, her hands covering her face. Nicky wrapped his arms around her as Rio leaned in and the moment Agatha’s hands fell away she kissed her lips. Rio’s face was momentarily stunned when she realized she hadn’t asked if she could in front of Nicky, she relaxed a second later when Agatha pulled her back in. 

 

The sound of Nicky gagging brought them back to the present. “Ew. Grown ups are weird.”

 

Agatha kept her hand on the back of Rio’s neck as she glared at her son. “You’re weird.”

 

He turned and pointed to the flowers. “Rio and me picked these for you! And we made a cake! And Rio got you a gift.”

 

Agatha smiled as she continued to cry. “Oh… that was… sweet.” Rio rubbed at her back as if sensing her need for touch in the moment, being proven right the moment Agatha leaned into her.

 

Rio pulled the chair back out and helped her settle into the seat. “My… darling.”

 

Agatha noticed the hesitation, as if Rio had meant to say something else, she let it go. Watching as her son pointed to the flowers and Rio recited their meanings. She placed the bag in Agatha’s hands as everyone sat around the table. Careful fingers removing the tissue paper with care. Blue eyes lighting up when she saw the stuffed bunny, bringing it up to hug it.

 

Nicky looked at Rio with a smirk. “Momma loves bunnies.” Rio wanted to fucking high five Billy for the impulse buy.

 

Agatha’s fingers dipped back in slowly and came away with a small rectangular box, her fingers hesitant to open it. Rio waited expectantly, holding her breath as she did. A thick deep purple watch with a silver face staring back at her. Rio took the watch from the box and turned around the device so Agatha could see the inscription. 

Agatha Harkness. The Forest. 2024.

 

Agatha’s fingers ghosted over the engraving. Her eyes lifted to Rio’s as they creased. Rio moved to fix it to her wrist as Nicky got out candles for the cake. Agatha’s lips quivered with words she didn’t know how to say when Rio took the offered lighter and lit the candles. “Make a wish, Agatha.”

 

The bright blue eyes shown with a happiness they had never known before as she closed her eyes, savoring the moment, then blew them out.

Chapter 24

Chapter Summary

short chapter, but don't worry, the next should come out tonight. :) A talk about finances and soon we will meet.... JEN! :D So excited for you all to get their backstory. my version of it at least.

CHAPTER 24 

 

Agatha sat on the couch with one knee up in the air. Her fingers dancing across the keyboard as her eyes took in the prices on the rentals around LA, she would be lucky if her and Nicky could even afford a studio in Sherman Oaks. Though she wondered if she could afford the gas because while the travel to the studio seemed like it shouldn’t take that long, every time she looked up the commute it was well over an hour. 

 

She chewed on her lip, about ready to bust it open when she heard Rio come in the front door. As her blue eyes looked up she noticed that the woman was preoccupied flipping through her mail. Agatha’s eyes went back to her laptop to continue falling into her panic when Rio plopped down on the couch beside her. 

 

“What are you looking at?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha shrugged, her teeth releasing her lip. “Just, trying to plan.”

 

Rio’s brown eyes took in the apartment search before her. “Ah, yeah those are… about right for the area. You don’t want to live there though, the commute is way too far.” She patted Agatha’s thigh as she stood. “Won’t be a good idea once you have fans either, way too accessible.”

 

Agatha watched her wander off to the kitchen before she herself closed her laptop and followed, trying to sound aloof and failing miserably.

 

“So… when… when do we get paid?” she crossed her arms and leaned against the doorway. 

 

Rio moved about grabbing some weed soda from a top shelf, turning, she handed one to Agatha. “Generally, a few months after filming. Usually a lump sum, but sometimes they put us on a payment schedule.”

 

She moved to wander towards the backyard when Agatha followed close behind. 

 

“So… how do people, live, while they wait for that money to come in?” Agatha was starting to wonder if this all was a good idea. From what she was understanding it seemed like she would be relying on Rio for quite some time, and she wasn’t sure how comfortable she was with that idea. She was growing nauseous.

CHAPTER 26 

Agatha had another photoshoot and Rio had offered to watch Nicky. She had felt confident about the decision until the moment her lover had left and she was left with brown eyes staring up at her. She noticed for the first time how much the boy looked like he was hers. Brown eyes, darker hair, his complexion more easily matched hers than his mother’s. She tried to ignore the special brand of anxiety that raced through her veins when she thought of Nicky being hers. She watched as he shifted from foot to foot smiling up at her. 

 

“Can we have snacks?”

Rio sighed. She could do this. Kids were just smaller people. She liked Nicky, they always had an easy time together, she could totally do this. She moved to her fridge and opened it, staring off into the potential options inside. She assumed Agatha would probably prefer something healthy for her child. She contemplated if Nicky was old enough to think vegetables were a snack or a punishment.

 

She heard a ball bouncing and she saw Nicky with the soccer ball she had gotten for him and Ruffland to play with, the boy dribbling it with his feet. Rio’s fingers wove into the sheets. “I know it doesn’t make sense… but I’m getting older, Nicky, and women… can’t have babies forever… our… eggs, go away. I just wanted to make sure I saved a few. Just in case.”

 

Nicky’s arms loosened on himself slightly. “You’re not making a baby?” His voice turned hopeful.

 

Rio shook her head. “No, not right now.” She indicated his mother. “Your mom was helping me so it wouldn’t hurt me like it did her. And she is not your other mother, Nicky. She didn’t want me doing this.”

 

He chewed at his lip as he took in her words. Rio continued on. “Agatha is kind, Nicky. She’s a beautiful person, and I just want her to have everything she didn’t before. I know I’m not great at knowing what she needs, or what you need yet, but I want to learn.” Her voice trailed off. “And I never want to hurt you, either of you.”

 

She heaved in a breath. “I started a new medication and was not very nice to your Mom today, and yet, she still wanted to help me.” Rio shrugged. “I was having a bad day. It wasn’t her fault.” She tried to keep her tears from falling. “Please, don’t yell at her because of me. She didn’t do anything wrong.”

 

Nicky’s little hands shook. “I just found you, Rio. I don’t want to lose you.” He rubbed his face on his sleeve.

 

Rio sighed. “You won’t lose me, buddy. You and your mom are taking great care of me. I’m alright.” She leaned on her arm looking down at her stomach. “Would you like to help me, too? That way you can see nothing bad is going to happen.”

 

Nicky’s eyes appeared from behind his arm. Rio patted the bed and Nicky moved to sit beside her, her arm coming around him. “What if… we explain everything that’s happening. You’re a big kid, and very smart, I know you can understand.”

 

Nicky nodded. “I’m almost seven,”

 

Rio smiled, “Yeah, that’s a big age.” She pointed at the needles. “Those are a medication that is supposed to help get the eggs to come out. So that maybe, one day, they could make a baby. Because if I don't take them out, all my eggs will just disappear.”

 

Nicky sighed. “You don’t want to be a mom.” 

 

Rio nodded. “Yeah, I don’t. But I get scared sometimes that I might change my mind. So, I just wanted to save a few eggs. Do you think that would be okay?” Dark eyes watched as Nicky thought about things. “If this really upsets you, I will stop.”

 

Nicky looked at Rio’s stomach again. “Momma’s not going to hurt you?”

 

Rio shook her head. “No. She’s not. Not like your other mom hurt her.”

 

The kid’s shoulders deflated. Little brown eyes looked at Agatha as she stood frozen. Seeming like she very much wanted to rip out her own heart. “Momma?”

 

Blue eyes met her son’s. “I promise I won’t hurt her, Nicky. I really… care about her.”

 

Nicky extended his hand for Agatha and she quickly moved to take the offering before her child could take it away again. Nicky looked to the space next to him and at Rio. 

 

Agatha sat carefully as if she wasn’t sure she was really allowed to be there.

 

Nicky sighed. “I’m sorry, Momma. You’re… not mommy. I know that.” He looked up, seeming disappointed in himself. “I just got scared.” He moved to hug her and Agatha wrapped her arms around him tight. 

 

“I’m sorry, baby. You shouldn’t have found out this way.”

 

Rio’s hand lifted to Agatha’s back, holding her lightly. Nicky looked between them. His face, thoughtful. “Is… Rio going to be my new mom?”

 

Agatha’s mouth dropped open and Rio smiled. “Let’s not give your mom a heart attack, kid. Let’s leave that talk for another day.”

 

Agatha held on to Nicky, worried he would never willingly enter her arms again, when the kid cuddled into her. “I just feel like we would make a good family.”

 

Rio tapped at his arm. “Hey, we are a family. Even if we are different than all the others you see, there’s no right way to be a family.” He nodded, nuzzling into his momma.

 

Agatha’s eyes looked into Rio’s over her son. Though she couldn’t tell her yet, this was everything she had always wanted.

CHAPTER 33 

 

Agatha’s eyes were a bit bloodshot from her lack of sleep. She had been up all night worrying about Rio’s procedure. The woman waved her off that it was just minor surgery and that she would be just fine, and for Agatha to stop panicking because that was freaking her out. 

 

Agatha had been so tightly wound that Nicky had to drag her away from the waiting room. He held her hand as they wandered over to a window with bushes. “Should we get Rio flowers?” Nicky’s brown eyes took in the colors outside.

 

Agatha’s hand gripped his back, trying not to think of her lover coding in surgery. She knew it wasn’t likely but accidents did happen. She ran her hand through Nicky’s hair. “That’s a good idea.” 

 

Nicky moved to grab Rio’s phone, unlocking it and texting Billy, Agatha’s eyes narrowing. “You know Rio’s password?”

 

Nicky’s eyes widened in alarm. “Uh, maybe?”

 

Agatha leaned in, her arms crossing. “Did you watch her open it?”

 

He nodded. “Yeah. Billy got your flowers. I figured he could help us. Since we have to wait here for Rio and all.”

 

Agatha shifted her weight into her left hip. She opened her phone and checked her bank account before locking the device. “I have some money left, we could pay him back…”

 

Nicky brightened. “What kind of flowers?” His little eyes staring at the screen as he typed away. He bounced up and down as he got a reply. “Billy is free! He said he can head to the florist now, what did we want?”

 

Agatha opened her phone and searched for strange flowers . Rio did have a unique taste. Her eyes crinkled as they landed on a flower. “What about these, Nicky, it says they attract butterflies.”

 

His brown eyes studied the image, Agatha for the first time noticed how he and Rio had the exact same eye color. If she didn’t know, she would have assumed that her son had Rio’s DNA and not hers. She wondered what the odds of that were before she came back to herself, waiting on his response on the suggested flowers.

 

Nicky nodded. “I like them. I think Rio will too.”

 

Agatha’s mind drifted to her favorite flower and she tapped Nicky’s shoulder. “Have him add black roses.”

 

***

 

Agatha was pacing the waiting room when Billy arrived, her eyes landing on the young man who still looked like a teenager, as if he had just walked out of a Hot Topic with his mom. She smiled and held up her phone. “How much do I owe you?”

 

Billy waved her off, “Please, you’re keeping my boss busy and happy. That’s enough for me…” He scratched at the back of his neck. “Eddie says thank you.”

 

Agatha’s eyebrow lifted. “Who’s Eddie?”

 

Billy blushed. “My boyfriend.”

 

She nodded. “Well, I’m glad you two are able to enjoy more time together, but I would really like to pay you for these. I would like to give them to her, just from me, if that’s okay?” 

 

Billy rolled his eyes. “They were like eighty something. Keep the change out of it.”

 

Agatha snorted, shaking her head good naturedly. “I’ll get it out of you eventually.” She typed out eighty in the cash app and hit send. 

 

Billy narrowed his eyes. “Would like to see you try.” His gaze landed on Nicky and he waved. “Hello.”

 

Nicky waved back. “Thank you for helping us.”

 

Billy saluted him. “Anytime, Rio’s kinda the best. I had no idea she was having a procedure done. I hope she’s okay?”

 

Agatha pursed her lips and shrugged. “It’s nothing serious, it’s for vanity.” An instant later wanting to facepalm as she made it sound like Rio was either having her nose done or a boob job.

 

Billy scoffed, his hand coming to his chest scandalized. “Wow, I had no idea that she… well, she looked great before, I’m sure whatever she decided on will be good too.” He waved awkwardly as he departed. “You two give her all of my best and let me know if you need anything else!”

 

Agatha held the vase of flowers awkwardly and Nicky leaned over to smell them. “I love roses,” 

 

His mother smiled softly. “I love them too.”

 

***

 

Rio’s eyes were drifting as she came in and out. She groaned and Agatha’s chest physically hurt. She had flagged down the nurse more than once to try and get them to give her something when they assured her that if she woke up telling them things hurt, then they would deal with it. Agatha didn’t like their lack of preparation and it was up to Nicky to keep her calm. 

 

Rio’s hand rubbed at her stomach, the small incision clearly noticed even as her mind hadn’t caught back up yet. Her eyes staring longingly at Agatha. “You’re here?”

 

Agatha sat at her hip, and cleared her fallen hair from her face as the woman tried to pull her closer. “Dear… you need to not pull on your incision. I’m not going anywhere.” She eased Rio back down and noticed her pout.

 

 “I want you to hold me.”

 

Agatha rolled her eyes. “We can discuss that once we get home.”

 

Nicky leaned onto the bed. “Hey, Rio!”

 

The woman smiled lazily. “Hey, Nicks.” She looked up and stared at the flowers. Nicky turning and pointing. “We got you flowers! Billy helped. Me and Mom choose which ones.”

 

Rio’s eyes softened before they scrunched, her hand coming to cover her mouth as she suppressed her laughter. Wincing a moment later at the pull she must have felt in her abdomen. 

 

Nicky’s face scrunched as he looked to his mom to explain what was happening.

 

Agatha raised her arms, shrugging. “I think she’s still drugged.”

 

Rio shook her head. “No… Well, yes, but that’s not why I’m laughing.” She pointed lazily at the flowers. “Those are the ones I wanted to get for you, too.” She snickered. 

 

Agatha took them in thoughtfully. “Black roses are my favorite, I’ve always found them striking.”

 

Rio snorted. Her mind still reeling with her own knowledge, information that, without a filter, she decided to share. “They mean death.”

 

Blue eyes shot to her. “Come again?”

 

Rio looked up innocently at her as she nodded. “Yep, Billy told me when I tried to order them for you.” Her head tilted towards the other flowers as well. “Well, that’s not good.”

 

Agatha face-palmed. “What isn't? These attract butterflies. What do you have against butterflies?” She was flushing with embarrassment over her choices. Of course Rio would have a special interest in flowers, it was just her luck. 

 

Rio closed her mouth. “Oh. Okay, I won’t say anything.”

 

Nicky tapped on her arm without the IV. “Rio, I wanna know. What do they mean?”

 

Rio’s eyes looked at Agatha. “I’m not mad. Can I tell him what it means? It’s just flower meanings anyway. It’s all made up…”

 

Agatha let her face fall into her hand as she swept the other forward as if to tell her fine go ahead, embarrass her and ruin her son’s innocence .

 

Rio whispered loudly. “Those mean let me go . But if you meant that I don’t think you would be here, so I think this is all some type of misunderstanding.”

 

Agatha huffed. “Great.”

 

Rio smiled. She giggled into her pillow, her eyes fixating on the flowers. “I like them.”

 

Nicky smiled and Agatha snorted. “You would, you freak.”

 

Rio’s eyes widened, looked at Nicky, then back at Agatha, misunderstanding her use of the term. “We can’t talk about the couch stuff in front of him!”

 

Agatha blanched. “What? No, I didn’t mean….Uh. Nicky, close your ears.”

 

Nicky tilted his head. “I can’t actually close my ears, Mom.” When he received a glare, he covered them.

 

Agatha leaned close to Rio’s face. “No couch gymnastics until you’re better.”

 

Rio smirked. “But after?”


Agatha shrugged. “We can talk about it.”

Chapter Summary

Some more fuzzy feelings with Rio's post op :)

CHAPTER 34

Agatha kept watch over Rio in her room. There was no way she was taking Rio up to hers with the way she hissed every time her abdomen stretched, pulling on her new incision.

 

Agatha had tried to keep busy tidying up the space, but in the end she had done little since Nicky went to bed, aside from sit and keep watch over Rio. The woman in question had been relatively peaceful since arriving home. Only occasionally groaning and asking for more pain meds. Agatha kept a sharp eye on the clock and the pills were kept in the kitchen. 

 

She pushed fluids every time Rio was awake and it was just about time to wake her up to go to the bathroom. Her eyes watching the shadows in the room, as if something was about to walk out of them and show her something to really be scared of. Like taking Rio away. Her mind was starting to wander to waking nightmares with such little sleep, but the moment she heard Rio waking up, her fears shattered.

 

“Agatha?”

 

She moved closer from her position in the chair. “Honey, I’m here. What did you need?”

 

Dark eyes found her without much of an issue. The woman in bed sighed, taking in Agatha sitting before her. “Why don’t you sleep in my room?”

 

Blue eyes scrunched in confusion. “Because I have my own room.”

 

Rio’s eyebrows furrowed. “That was a dumb idea on my part.”

 

Agatha snorted. “It’s fine.” She moved to brush her hand through Rio’s hair, the woman leaning into the touch. “If we shared a room, you would miss out on all the fun of sneaking into my room at night.”

 

Rio grabbed Agatha’s hand. “My room is right upstairs… you could just as easily…”

 

Agatha leaned against some pillows. “Nicky is down here, what if he gets scared?”

 

Rio took a moment to contemplate Agatha’s concerns before speaking, clearly becoming more self aware and less medicated. “I have no problem with him slipping into my bed…we’ve… already all slept in yours.” Rio's teeth dug into her lip. “Were you not alright with that?”

 

Agatha cupped Rio’s face gently, letting her thumb move back and forth across Rio’s cheek. “It made me happy that Nicky felt comfortable enough to climb into bed with you there.”

 

Rio sighed, relaxing again. “Then let me move in here with you.” Her eyes were pleading. “Though, just remember, I have a bigger bathroom…”

Agatha let her eyes fall to the mattress. “My bathroom is already set up…”

 

Rio rolled her eyes. “I can make room. And we can go slow. This room and your precious bathroom aren't going anywhere.”

 

Blue eyes scanned the desk. “I like drawing in here, that spot has really good lighting.”

 

Rio tried to scoot closer to Agatha and hissed, her hand went to her stomach but not before Agatha found it first. 

 

“Rio, be careful.” Her voice was firm and the dark haired woman rolled her eyes.

 

“It’s a small incision, it’s not going to kill me if I rip it open.”

 

Agatha glared. “No twisting and let’s not test that theory.”

 

Rio let her head fall back dramatically before she rolled her head to the side. “Move in with me, baby.”

 

Agatha snorted, her eyes lifting. “I already live with you.”

 

Rio shrugged. “Keep this room as your office. Just… sleep in mine.”

 

Agatha blew out a breath. “You can’t even get up to your room right now.”

 

Rio nodded. “For a couple days.” She worried her lip. “Would you let me stay in here with you? If you decided you really didn’t want to stay in my room?”

 

Blue eyes looked about the room. “I think… we could figure that out.” She laid back on the pillow, her face looking up at the ceiling. “This is starting to feel awfully domestic.” She swallowed back down the bile that threatened to come up her throat. “What if I’m not ready for… all of that?”

 

Rio reached for her hand but let her eyes also stray to the ceiling. “We try one night at a time. If you need your space… you take it. I won’t be mad.” She sighed. “I miss you when you’re not in bed with me.”

 

Agatha turned on her side, facing Rio, her eyes taking her in. Things with Rio just seemed easy . She wondered why that was. It was like Rio seemed in tune with her, every little touch or reassurance came right when she needed it. Agatha couldn’t understand why Rio even wanted to make the effort, why she chose to love her when there were so many other women on the planet. Her mind wandered and she didn’t exactly mean to blurt out her question, but once it was out she found that she did really want to hear Rio’s answer. “Why did you want me?”

 

Rio turned her face to Agatha, glaring at her. “Are you trying to get information out of me because I’m high?”

 

Agatha shrugged, a smile tugging at her lips. “Maybe?”

 

Rio smiled. “Well,” Her face shifted into a look of concentration. “I was working on that Thirst Post interview and I was reading a lot of… questionable comments,”

 

Agatha cringed. 

 

Rio lifted her arm to hold out her hand for Agatha's as it had slipped away; the woman took it in record time.

 

“I got to yours and… your photo.” She whistled. “Damn, honey, your eyes, your face… your nose, your lips, your… hands.” She sighed then giggled like a little girl. “Then the thing you said about the couch?” She groaned lightly. “It was just everything. You were beautiful, sexy… and already into me.”

 

Before Agatha could form words, Rio continued. “I went to your page right away and started to flip through your photos. I hadn’t seen your art account, and you hadn’t posted in a long time, but your photos, the pictures of you laughing and smiling… I felt like there was just this warmth to you that was infectious. I knew I would be missing you forever if I didn’t shoot my shot.”

 

Agatha bit her lip. “And what did you think when we… met?”

 

Rio smirked, a bit mischievous. “You were so nervous.” She played with Agatha’s fingers as her mind traveled backwards in time. “I honestly thought you were going to faint.”

 

Agatha sighed, feeling her chest flush. “I was.”

 

Rio nodded. “Yeah, I barely got the ice in time. Could have used it as an excuse for a daring rescue though, now that I think about it. But I gotta say, you did handle it pretty well.”

 

Blue eyes took in Rio’s face and how happy she was.

 

“The way you talked about Nicky, that really hit me. The way you… took something that hurt you so badly like your time with Tori, and made it beautiful instead with the family you have with Nicky, that made my heart want you more. You’re a survivor, Agatha. You’re so strong.” She laughed quietly. “Plus, the sounds you make when you get wet are unholy .”

 

Agatha scoffed and smacked Rio on the shoulder, her body vibrating from the love Rio poured over her so easily and how she soothed the discomfort of too many sentimental feelings with her humor. 

 

Agatha hummed. “Fine. I’ll… share a bed with you. For now.”

 

Rio smirked. “Is it because you don’t want to trek up to my room tonight, nor sleep on the couch?”

 

Agatha deadpanned. "Yes, because you obviously have nothing to do with it.”

 

Rio beamed. “Of course, we can’t have that.” She let her fingers drift to Agatha’s pulse. Agatha swallowed thickly as Rio closed her eyes and focused on her heart beating.

 

“I love this feeling. It reminds me that you’re real and that you’re actually here.”

 

Agatha closed her eyes. “I am here. For…” She felt her heart speed up as she ventured to make a confession. “For as long as you want me to be.”

 

Rio nodded. “And if I want you forever?”


Agatha felt like she might faint or throw up, it was a very good thing she was already laying down. “Then I guess I’m stuck with you forever.”

Chapter 35

Chapter Summary

Agatha takes a big swing and asks for something from the show's writer. Will she get it? Also, for as much as I these lesbians (and am a nb lesbian myself) it was fitting to have a bi character also enter the scene :) I hope she surprises you. <3 I had a lot of fun writing her hollywood love story.

And yes I wrote this months before I knew The Studio was even a thing.

CHAPTER 35: Sharon Davis 

 

Sharon Davis hadn’t done much since Mr. Davis died. She had retreated from her role as an executive at Monument. While many men in her position simply postured and got blowjobs all day long, Sharon had always been passionate about what they created. Stories that touched people on a deeper level. Stories that not only inspired others, but made some realize they did have a heart. It was how she had met Mr. Davis in the first place.

 

He had been such a grouchy middle aged man. While Sharon had been a rising star in the industry due to her own parents’ connections. She had crossed paths with him multiple times before they were trapped at a horribly dull work event together. Sharon had been sitting next to him when she decided he wasn’t worth her concern, and she had started to write her latest script idea on a napkin, Mr. Davis’s eyes wandered over to peek at her notes.

 

His eyes had widened as he read on, shocked that Sharon was a gifted storyteller, and not just another suit spinning corporate jargon. He had made her jump when he leaned in further to continue to read when she had adjusted her napkin further away. Both nearly having a heart attack as their eyes connected. They had both burst out laughing, and when someone across the table had too much to drink and knocked over their water, Mr. Davis snatched up Sharon’s script to save it. Sharon was head over heels ever since.

 

Mr. Davis was also the first person she had told that she was bisexual. In a time when being gay meant you had a disease of the mind, he quietly confessed he was as well. The couple had an instant connection over their love of stories as well as their queerness. They soon teamed up as angel investors for queer productions all over Hollywood. Hopeful that one day something would make it to Monument’s doorsteps and they could push it through. Sadly, Mr. Davis hadn’t lived to see the day.

 

They had a wonderful forty years together. Mr. Davis one rainy day had a stroke on his way home from work, and that had been the end of it. Luckily, he had written a letter to be given to Sharon should anything happen to him and his thoughtful words were one of the only reasons she didn’t completely fall apart. He encouraged her to continue to push for their dreams. That something she wrote needed to be seen by the world. 

 

This had sent her ripping through her greatest works like a person consumed by madness. She went through all of her husband's notes on her manuscripts until she found the perfect one. A show about queer witches. Ex-wives. Something that even the straight audience could understand. 

 

Over the years their paychecks and investments had amounted to a sum that Sharon could do just about anything she wanted. But going out on such a limb with the hard earned money the two had set aside had her pushing the studio to finance the project with a measly budget. 

 

She figured, should it become what she wanted, she would dump a good deal of her riches into the marketing. First, she just needed to make sure she struck gold. As she ripped through editing, she tried to envision who could bring her main character to life. She needed someone unexpected, known, with a strong occult following, but not so big that she couldn’t reach them. 

 

She spent the next six months pouring over tv shows and movies, driving herself insane trying to see each and every actress as her star. None were right – until she saw Rio Vidal’s work. She had seen her before but had forgotten about her. The last time she had seen her work was ten years ago, some small support role in a school drama. She watched as Rio’s acting had matured, how she had the depth now that Sharon was looking for. 

 

Sharon read the script, hearing it in Rio’s voice loud and clear, also seeing places where she should adjust the wordings to really capture Rio’s quirkiness. She could be funny, she could be dramatic. She could make you cry and want to rip your heart out with just a look. That, was her star.

 

She had found Lilia quickly enough. At first when she reached out and she had played it coy, knowing the woman must be shitting herself to be hearing from her. Then as she felt the energy building at Monument, her team agreeing to give Sharon her little show with some unknown writer and producer, she went in for the kill.

 

Lilia had been ecstatic, ready to bend over backwards for Sharon, not that the woman minded that image, Lilia had certainly been her type at one point in her life. She had met with her one Friday afternoon to discuss the logistics of the show, and her own secret involvement. Lilia, as a queer woman herself, was overjoyed with her little plot.

 

Sharon hadn’t expected Rio to ask for anything. But in the end, she was so glad she did because it had landed Agatha Harkness in her inbox. The woman’s acting was as natural as breathing, and a complete unknown would mean they could meet their budget easily. Her offers weren’t the best of the best, but she knew Rio’s offer was in line with around what the woman was making nowadays, well, almost. And she made Agatha a similar offer. Her mind was not sitting in the details of how she felt that all made sense.

 

She had been checking emails about how everything was shaping up on set when she saw an unusual email from Lilia Calderu appear in her inbox.

 

“Request from Agatha Harkness”

 

She pursed her lips. It was a bit late in the game for the unknown actor to be making requests at all. She opened the email to find a quick forward by Lilia before she opened a letter from Agatha herself.

 

To Our Fabulous Writer Producer and Team,

 

Hi, my name is Agatha Harkness. I know you must know me from my audition tapes, and first of all thank you so much for seeing this witch in me. I am truly grateful and this role is about to change my life. I find this role to be incredibly fulfilling as an actor, she is quite the challenge, as well as at times, I feel I am on a healing journey of my own through her eyes. 

 

What I wanted to ask is if there were any way we could do table reads for a few of the episodes we have left, in particular for the major ex-wives scenes. I have found that at times I have not been able to give everything I want to give to the scene for fear of the mental health of my fellow scene partners. I know it is our job to adjust our emotions to be believable on screen, but this at times can leave a toll on us performers when it is not properly prepared for. And in corporate terms, this affects the budget in delays. If we are able to do our homework together, for lack of a better term, I know we can finish with making this the groundbreaking piece it was meant to be. I myself as a queer woman have cried many times reading over the script and finally seeing myself so clearly in something. 

 

I’m not requesting that we do table reads for every episode or scene going forward, or that the table reads would need to be in person, but even just a remote workshop of the bigger scenes would be much appreciated. Again, I love the two main characters with my whole heart and I hope I am bringing justice to your vision.

 

With the utmost respect,

Agatha Harkness

 

Sharon sat back in her chair with a smile. She hadn’t thought about any of this from the point of view of the performers before. She had never been this close to something she had written, usually passing it off as an unknown writer and handing it to a trusted producer. She had a co-producer for this project that sat on site and reported back, but this letter from one of her actors was eye opening. She figured there was space in the timeline to work in a few remote table reads, she could approve that. They were halfway through filming and she really wanted to amp up the piece because if all went well, she was totally submitting this for award season.

 

She wrote some notes, and made some calls. Agatha Harkness was getting those table reads.
